mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">许晓琴</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New minor-fareast;">许秀云、<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">许艳</span></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">许章清</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、许志永<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">薛爱梅、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">薛桂云</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">薛丽威</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、薛莲霞、<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">薛少强</span>、薛玉春</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">希尔扎提•巴吾东：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">维吾尔族。<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年出生于新疆和田。历任新疆维吾尔自治区司法厅长、区党委政法委副书记，新疆维吾尔自治区政协副秘书长。据中国官媒报道，他被指控以中共党员领导干部身份为掩护，长期策划实施分裂国家活动，投靠“东伊运”组织，向境外人员非法提供情报。还将自己受贿所得<span lang="EN-US">120</span>万元和一套房产送给“东伊运”组织使用。并且为服刑人员提供庇护，故意隐瞒服刑人员脱逃的事实，包庇嫌疑人。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日首次披露以“分裂罪”判处希尔扎提•巴吾东死刑缓期二年。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">夏东梅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河南省项城市法轮功学员，女。夏东梅于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被警察抓捕，并关押在周口市看守所。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">2023</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，河南省周口市川汇区法院庭审法轮功学员夏东梅。后川汇区法院判处夏东梅有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金五千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/3/11/457628.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/3/11/457628.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">夏洪民：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北涞水县法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">1956</span>年生，保定市涞水县涞水镇东关村人。曾是建筑工人。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日因宣传法轮功事被抓捕。先被行政拘留、后转刑事拘留，后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/5/24/461195.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/5/24/461195.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">夏霖：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1970</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US"> 9</span>月<span lang="EN-US"> 15</span>日出生，贵州省人，北京市华一律师事务所合伙人，维权律师。曾因为人公义正派、代理案件认真有效而在业界有较高知名度；近年来，曾代理过包括艾未未、冉云飞等案在内的多起敏感维权案件；<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月—<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，曾为北京市小贩崔英杰杀死城管李志强案做免费辩护律师；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，曾为刺死官员女服务员邓玉娇涉嫌故意杀人案做代理律师；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，曾与人权律师浦志强一起为地震义工谭作人辩护；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年人权律师浦志强被中共当局抓捕时，曾为其备选辩护人之一；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，因其为北京传知行社会经济研究所负责人郭玉闪被捕案担任辩护人而被北京市警方突然从家中带走，随后被以涉嫌“赌博”和“诈骗”罪刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日又被以涉嫌“诈骗罪”正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日其案被移送检察院审查起诉，但因证据不足曾被延期三次；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被该法院经一审以“诈骗罪”重判<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年，剥权<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">12</span>万元。其不服上诉。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，经北京第二中级法院二审改判为有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。目前仍被关押在北京市第一看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">夏忆林：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">山西太原法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1954</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共集团开始迫害法轮功后，两次被判刑，刑期分别为<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月再次被抓捕构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年底夏忆林家人收到监狱方电话通知才知已被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年半。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/5/%E6%9B%BE%E4%B8%A4%E6%AC%A1%E9%81%AD%E5%86%A4%E7%8B%B1%E8%BF%AB%E5%AE%B3-%E5%A4%AA%E5%8E%9F%E5%A4%8F%E5%BF%86%E6%9E%97%E5%8F%88%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-434383.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">夏泽红</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：安徽淮南市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年生，原来是淮南潘二矿职工。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日晚发法轮功资料人时，被国保警察抓捕，并把资料和电瓶车推走。在未出示任何证件的情况下，警察非法抄了她的家。后一审被判<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，上诉，近悉，淮南市中院改为<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">向德斌：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">湖北省咸宁市人，咸宁市咸安区个体出租司机，法轮功学员。因信仰和宣传法轮功备受当局打压迫害，经常被骚扰、跟踪监控。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被咸宁市通城县警方抓捕，之后被送进湖北省法制教育所板桥洗脑班关押，并被进行强行性思想转化迫害。同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，被转入咸宁市咸安区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日上午，咸安区法院对向德斌非法庭审，但没有结果。向德斌仍然一直被非法关押在咸安区看守所，至今已经<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年多。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">向冬：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">云南省昆明市法轮功学员，女。原是昆明市某房地产公司的高管。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年四十多岁，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年她因发法轮功资料被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年。向冬女士这次是因修炼法轮功遭人举报。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被当局抓捕，随后被关押到昆明市看守所。之后西山区国保大队伙同西山区检察院、西山区法院对向冬司法构陷，最后将她判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。这是向冬第二次遭中共邪党法院判刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/6/23/%E4%BA%91%E5%8D%97%E6%98%86%E6%98%8E%E5%B8%82%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E5%90%91%E5%86%AC%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4-445304.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/6/23/%E4%BA%91%E5%8D%97%E6%98%86%E6%98%8E%E5%B8%82%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E5%90%91%E5%86%AC%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4-445304.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">向祚华</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日出生，湖北省宜昌市秭归县人，宜昌市秭归县九畹溪镇砚窝台村二组（原芝兰乡芦池湾村三组）村民，冤狱受害人，维权举报人，中国在押维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年向柞华来因家人与邻居纠纷被宜昌市秭归县警方抓走，并被以涉嫌“故意伤害罪”拘捕；<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，其被湖北省宜昌市秭归县法院一审以同罪名判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年；其不服，当庭表示上诉；同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，因其向宜昌市中级法院递交了附有新证人名单的刑事上诉状，之后虽经二审，但仍一直不被宣判，直至其在湖北宜昌监狱服刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年之后，才将将维持一审判决的二审裁定书交给本人；其不服屡屡申诉，且其辩护律师也将数份足以证明一审判决存在认定事实不清的现场证人证言提交给各级司法部门，但都被耽延未审；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">出狱后，因其为讨公道而不惜长期举报、投诉因司法不公被冤狱，然而截至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年，最高法院、最高检察院以及宜昌市中级法院均对其申诉驳回请求，以致于其不得不通过网络寻求社会正义力量的关注与支持；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，因当局要确保中共“二十大”顺利召开，其遂被秭归县警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，至今未放。目前被羁押于湖北省秭归县看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/09/20.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/09/20.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">项本子：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">工作在广东深圳，原籍湖北省麻城市的法轮功学员。因修炼法轮功，曾经两次在福建省被分别判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半和<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日下午，在广东省深圳市住宿处，被广东省东莞市长安区乌沙派出所警察，联合广东省国保和东莞市国保，抓捕。项本子被关押在东莞市第<span lang="EN-US">2</span>看守所。据说是因两个月前，项本子在东莞市长安区发放大法法轮功资料，被监控和跟踪。后遭东莞市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，项本子被关押到广东省韶关市北江监狱迫害。之后，家人多次向北江监狱提出会见，监狱方以项本子是法轮功学员，是严管期，不可会见。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">项逢选：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1975</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，浙江省台州市仙居县朱溪镇小园村人，网名“皓月”，广州市某洗衣店业主，维权公民，新公民运动参与者。早年因年少气盛，好打抱不平，曾做出过违法行为而被抓捕判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。出狱后前往广东谋生，并在亲友帮助下在广州珠海区开设一家洗衣店。因为人慷慨，极富同情心，经常接济社会底层群众，体会到无钱看病、上学、买房等国计民生问题给普通百姓造成的困惑和巨大压力，遂积极探索社会改革和新公民运动之路。此期间，与张六毛等多位维权人士结成志同道合好友，并经常参与街头围观、抗争声援；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月因在多个<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>群中以“皓月”网名积极宣传“要通过武装暴动改变现有体制，走民主宪政之路”，并成立“民选党”，遂遭到广州市当局的疯狂打压；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日与张六毛、苏东亮等多人一同被广州珠海区警方抓捕，张六毛当时被以涉“寻衅滋事”罪由刑拘，而其被涉“颠覆国家政权罪”刑拘；后被广州市天河区检察院正式批捕，被指控“要以武力推翻现在政权”，“正在制造爆炸物准备搞破坏，对公共安全构成严重的现实危害”。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，张六毛被酷刑致死于广州市第三看守所，而其一直没有音信。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日获悉，其已被广州市中级法院以“制造炸弹危害公共安全案主犯”重判。此前被羁押于广州市天河区看守所，目前服刑监狱不详。具体刑期不详，只知刑期很长。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">项锦锋：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">福建维权人士。项锦锋长期帮助和关注弱势群体维权。曾在<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月、<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月被当地国保带走问话，原因涉及他所建的微信群经常谈论政治敏感话题，以及他对公民维权的关注。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，项锦锋在厦门高崎机场海关被限制出境，并被剪掉护照。项锦峰还曾于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日连续<span lang="EN-US">2</span>天被辖区警方传讯，主要调查他在网上发表的“六四”言论，此后项锦峰所在的“风花雪月群”被封杀。项锦锋约于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被拘留在老家龙岩市连城县看守所，涉嫌罪名不详，可能与其网上言论有关。其父母没有收到拘留通知书，只到朋口镇派出所签了字。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/09/blog-post_23.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/09/blog-post_23.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">肖传雄：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">福建省宁德市法轮功学员。曾因信法轮功并参与网上法轮功信息资料接受、传送、现金转帐及宣传等活动，而被宁德市国保人员长期跟踪、蹲点监控。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月底—<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月下旬，肖传雄与金丽燕、陈星光、王田等<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人先后被宁德市警方从家中抓捕，各人家庭被查抄。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，肖传雄被宁德市检察院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”正式批捕。据悉，肖传雄因信法轮功曾已被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并与杨雄一起被关押在福建省龙岩监狱服刑，惨遭狱警残害。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，其一行<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人被福建省宁德市蕉城区法院以“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”分别非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>—<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年不等，其中，肖传雄被重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元；目前都被关押于福建省宁德市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月底。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/12/12_23.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/12/12_23.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">肖春：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">男，<span lang="EN-US">80</span>后，四川达州公民，长期在福建南安工作生活。热心公义，多年来坚持传播常识，致力推动社会进步，构建公民社会。因<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日在厦门大学门口拉横幅呼吁释放许志永、黄琦、李怀庆、王臧、余文生、程渊、丁家喜、张展等良心犯。并宣传人权、民主、法治等理念，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日被福建省南安是警方抓捕。在没有通知家属的情况，被当局以“寻衅滋事”的名义秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，截止目前家属都未曾收到判决书。肖春已于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日移送至福建省漳州监狱服刑。目前其夫人需要照顾家里的<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个孩子和一个老人，成了家里唯一的顶梁柱，一家人生活十分拮据。漳州监狱已疫情为由，停止会见，无奈家属只能写信。但信寄出逾三个月了，没有任何回音，家属非常挂念并担心肖的身体，呼吁当局保障肖春通信等基本权利。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">肖德玉：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖南益阳市法轮功学员，女，别名肖德英，<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年生，湖南省益阳市赫山区欧江岔人。她一直在湖南长沙打零工为生。肖德玉一九九八年开始修炼法轮功。因坚持修炼法轮功，遭中共当局多次迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日凌晨一点多钟被长沙市开福区刑警队在其居住的出租房抓捕，并抄家构陷，关押到长沙第四看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月获刑，她已经被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/09/16_27.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/09/16_27.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/9/2/%E6%B9%96%E5%8D%97%E7%9B%8A%E9%98%B3%E5%B8%82%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%82%96%E5%BE%B7%E7%8E%89%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-464848.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/9/2/%E6%B9%96%E5%8D%97%E7%9B%8A%E9%98%B3%E5%B8%82%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%82%96%E5%BE%B7%E7%8E%89%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-464848.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">萧亮：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">江西省南昌市人，网络活跃人士，常用推特号：<span lang="EN-US">@xiaoliang999</span>，南昌画家，异见表达者，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，因中共二十大前夕，有“四通桥勇士”彭立发（网名彭载舟）在北京四通桥上悬挂倒习横幅，指责习近平是独裁者，要求他下台，随后即被抓捕；此事件一经传播，很快促使国内外许多华人站出来表达他们的对彭载舟先生的支持。此期间，萧亮因画了一幅四通桥勇士彭立发的画像并发到推特上，遂于<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日被江西省南昌市东湖区警方带走，家遭查抄，而后被以“寻衅滋事”为由行政拘留；但之后其很快又被警方以同罪由转为刑拘，同时，其妻子被问讯，主要涉及其有何嗜好，都交些什么朋友，有参加什么组织或收谁的钱等等问题，均被其妻子一一否定；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，其被南昌市东湖区检察院以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”予以批捕；截至当前，知其已有代理律师介入，且已与其会见两次，但其具体详情因警方一直拒透，故一概不清。目前疑似被羁押于南昌市第一看守所（南昌市新建县南昌警察学校<span lang="EN-US">100</span>米附近，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">210036</span>）。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/12/blog-post_95.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/12/blog-post_95.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">肖青山</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：江西省资深的维权人士。在肖青山的维权过程中，近年来多次举横幅要求江西省各级政法机关、及纪检监察机关依法惩治司法中的败类。因为其举横幅喊口号都有出处，也就是<span lang="EN-US">CCTV</span>无时不刻宣扬的那一套，公安国保多次希望他不要举这些横幅，尤其不要上网。从<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年“十一”前夕，肖青山就与外界失去了联系，无论朋友们怎样拨打其电话或微信留言，但肖青山的手机与微信始终无应答，朋友们几经周折，终于联系上其家人，证实其已被刑事拘留，目前关押在江西吉安市看守所。但家人不愿意透露更多信息。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2021</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，其家属获得的逮捕通知书，终于可以确认其是被吉安市公安局青山区分局国保以“涉嫌寻衅滋事罪”抓捕的事实<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。</b></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2023</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日获悉，肖青山被以“虚假诉讼罪”、“寻衅滋事罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。目前其已经从江西省吉安市看守所转监到江西省吉安市吉安监狱（通信地址：江西省吉安市吉州区<span lang="EN-US">1126</span>信箱）。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月底。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/10/blog-post_55.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/10/blog-post_55.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/11/blog-post_43.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/11/blog-post_43.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/03/46.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/03/46.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">肖树清：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">天津市北辰区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月因讲法轮功被人举报，曾多次被北辰区瑞景派出所抓捕：有时被劫持去法院；有时去检察院；有时去多个地方检查身体。每次都是经肖树清讲真相当天放回或几天后放回家。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，肖树清又被北辰瑞景派出所抓捕抽血、检查身体；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日再次被瑞景派出所抓捕，没有出示任何字据与凭证，说是“案子”还没结，准备开庭。晚上九点许，瑞景派出所口头通知家属：肖被以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施”判了<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，现被关押在北辰看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">肖艳芳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">湖北孝感市汉川市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，肖艳芳、刘义波、王四美、王庆、舒运兰等<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人到汉川市马鞍乡联洪村、天成村告诉村民法轮功遭迫害真相及避疫良方，被村民举报，遭马鞍派出所警察抓捕。第<span lang="EN-US">2</span>天，<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人因疫情原因被放回家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，汉川市公安局对肖艳芳、刘义波、王庆、王四美、舒运兰<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人下达「监视居住通知书」。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日肖艳芳、刘义波被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，汉川国保人员到湖南长沙，将流落在外打工的法轮功学员王庆抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，汉川市公安局分水派出所警察在分水镇抓捕了王四美和另一名法轮功学员胡汉姣。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月下旬，孝昌县法院作出判决，胡汉姣、王四美遭冤判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刘义波遭冤判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，肖艳芳遭冤判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，王庆遭冤判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。肖艳芳刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">肖永芬：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吉林省德惠市五台乡法轮功学员。孙桂昌和肖永芬夫妇各被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，已经于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月份被羁押到公主岭监狱和吉林省女子监狱。孙桂昌和妻子肖永芬<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被不法警察入室绑架。孙贵昌被送到德惠市拘留所非法拘留五天。肖永芬被送到长春第二看守所检查身体，不合格拒收，第二天下午<span lang="EN-US">7</span>点多钟放回家，被监视居住。后来，孙桂昌被非法关押德惠看守所。肖永芬因身体和精神状况被放回家，并被监视居住。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日左右，吉林省公安厅数个警察将在其女儿看家的肖永芬绑架。据悉，肖永芬以前在长春黑嘴子劳教所被迫害得精神失常，现在患有高血压和糖尿病（后期），脚部严重溃烂，现在被关押在吉林省女子监狱八监区；孙桂昌被关押在公主岭监狱九监区。多年来，上述两个监狱公开执法犯法，利用死人床、坐小板凳、长期剥夺睡眠、电棍电击、殴打、上绳等各种酷刑残害和转化善良无辜的法轮功学员，多人被迫害致伤、致残、致疯、致死。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">肖真义：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1970</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年代出生，重庆市人，重庆市两江新区大竹林康美小区公民，重庆市区镇级人大代表独立参选人（之一），重庆绿叶行动志愿者，人权捍卫者，中国在押维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，曾因以重庆市合法公民身份积极参选区镇级人大代表换届选举，故引发社会热议，并对其等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>位公民的“重庆人大参选独立侯选人联合宣言”给予高度评价和首肯，但终因仅是普通百姓，毫无官场背景或官场背景的支持，而被当地小区以“不合格”为由拒绝报名参选；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，曾因摄录和发布了一段有关当地农贸市场涉及疫情的小视频，而被所住大竹林康美小区派出所警方传唤，并将其手机等当场收走；曾因其未婚女友唐云淑因自家三处房产遭政府强拆损毁而不断维权，遂多次被送进精神病院和被刑拘及判刑，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日其女友又被警方拘捕，在超押<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多后，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日被重庆市丰都县法院以“寻衅滋事罪”重判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；此期间，其为营救女友四处奔波呼吁，后因不断为女友喊冤，并持续在网上发声寻求正义和声援，而亦被重庆市两江新区警方抓走失联；后经重庆友人钟声牛与朱春华多方打探，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，终于获知其被重庆市渝北区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”正式逮捕，至今其案已被法院秘密开庭两次，但尚未宣判；据悉，其二位重庆友人钟声牛与朱春华愿为其做代理辩护人，但遭法院拒绝。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">重庆市渝北区法院<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月以“寻衅滋事罪”判处肖真义有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月。肖真义不服，已提起上诉；二审正在等待中。目前肖真义被羁押于重庆市渝北区看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/02/210.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/02/210.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/blog-post_89.html"><b><span class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">谢桂芳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">甘肃省兰州市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1959</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">64</span>岁，原甘肃省嘉峪关市核工业<span lang="EN-US">404</span>厂退休职工。一九九六年五月，谢桂芳开始修炼法轮功，在中共自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月对法轮功的疯狂迫害中，谢桂芳坚持信仰，曾多次被中共抓捕、关押，在派出所、看守所、洗脑班、监狱遭受迫害。谢桂芳于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被兰州市七里河区警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月获悉：谢桂芳已被兰州市城关区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，现被关押在兰州第一看守所迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/8/16/%E5%B1%A1%E9%81%AD%E8%BF%AB%E5%AE%B3-%E7%94%98%E8%82%83%E5%85%B0%E5%B7%9E%E8%B0%A2%E6%A1%82%E8%8A%B3%E5%8F%88%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%BA%94%E5%B9%B4-464242.html"><b font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">谢汉奎：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东梅州市梅江区法轮功学员。因在一个微信群里提到一句话“为什么会有人类”，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日上午，谢汉奎遭梅江区警察抓捕、抄家，当天被释放回家；<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，谢汉奎再次被警察抓捕，并被刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，谢汉奎被逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，谢汉奎遭梅县区法院开庭。现获悉已被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。谢汉奎不服，提出上诉。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/10/26.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/10/26.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/9/29/%E4%B8%80%E5%8F%A5%E2%80%9C%E4%B8%BA%E4%BB%80%E4%B9%88%E4%BC%9A%E6%9C%89%E4%BA%BA%E7%B1%BB%E2%80%9D-%E8%B0%A2%E6%B1%89%E5%A5%8E%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%A4%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-466451.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/9/29/%E4%B8%80%E5%8F%A5%E2%80%9C%E4%B8%BA%E4%BB%80%E4%B9%88%E4%BC%9A%E6%9C%89%E4%BA%BA%E7%B1%BB%E2%80%9D-%E8%B0%A2%E6%B1%89%E5%A5%8E%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%A4%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-466451.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; text-decoration: none; text-underline: none;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">谢汉柱：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">男，<span lang="EN-US">1962</span>年生，原梅县农业局农村能源股副股长，工作屡受表彰奖励，是个优秀的国家公务员。一九九九年中共迫害法轮功后，他只因坚定修炼大法，即被劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日上午，谢汉柱的妻子被梅州市公安局梅江分局国保大队和城西派出所警察以其被人“举报”为由劫持回家，夫妻俩一同遭抓捕，并被抄家，抢走一些法轮功书籍和现金等私人财物。谢汉柱的妻子阿兰被拘留五天后回家，而谢汉柱则在之后遭逮捕，</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">2022</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，广东省梅州市梅县区法院在未通知家属和律师的情况下，采取视频方式开庭，对法轮功学员谢汉柱判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚金五万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/12/7/452834.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/12/7/452834.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">谢建新：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广西桂林市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日半夜，谢建新与妻子赵任远被桂林市七星分局的派出所警察声称“测体温”闯入家中，搜查抄走<span lang="EN-US">1</span>轮功书籍、资料、法轮功币等物品，并抓捕、构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被庭审，<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日均被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">谢俊彪：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1981</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日出生，四川省成都市人，住成都市双流区怡心街道青云寺小区<span lang="EN-US">7</span>组，维权公民，民主理念追求者，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年，曾因所在成都市双流区政府在未提供任何有效档，也未与当地村民达成拆迁补偿协议的前提下，便强征强拆、驱逐村民，令其及众村民个人权益严重受损，随在信访投诉无望情况下，走上了从成都到北京等地的维权抗争之路；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年，曾因多次在成都市和双流区的上访无果，而两次进京上访投诉，随数次遭双流区警方传唤及登门威胁警告；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，曾因习近平等中共高层常委将到成都市双流区视察，而遭双流区公兴派出所警方莫名破门辱骂和殴打，事后，又因其将此不幸经历和猜测发于微信群，爆料“明天可能有大爷到双流视察”，随旋即被双流区警方以“寻衅滋事”罪由行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，曾因再次进京信访、投诉喊冤，并在北京市西城区转发维权动态等信息，从而被北京警方视为传播 “敏感事件相关文章”，被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘于北京市西城区看守所<span lang="EN-US">37</span>天；后又因坚持关注“六四天网”创办人黄琦冤案，并积极参加营救活动，遂遭成都当局进一步打击，曾被双流区警方多次上门警告、传唤及行政拘留等；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，曾因在微信群中表达心声及民主要求，又被当局警告，称其“接受媒体采访，要重点稳控“；同年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，因其在四川省人大、政协两会召开之际，又到四川省人大外举牌，牌子上写：“戴表（代表）不为民作主不如回家抓老鼠”，随当天即被当地警方刑事拘留，一个月后获取保候审；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，在其面临取保候审一年期满之际，成都市双流区警方以“取保候审期间离开居住地“之名将其再度以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，家被搜查；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，知其被成都市双流区检察院以同罪名予以批捕，后其案宗被移送到成都市双流区法院；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，其案在双流区法院开庭审理，同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，终被该法院一审以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日；其不服，表示上诉，并称只要二审维持原判或改判即使一天的罪，即仍坚决申诉；据悉，羁押期间曾遭酷刑虐待，被狱警殴打并戴比“工字链”更严酷的戒具<span lang="EN-US">13</span>天。此前被羁押于成都市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，谢俊彪被送四川省眉山监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/02/26_15.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/02/26_15.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp;</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/12/26_15.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/12/26_15.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">谢清：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广东省江门市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，丈夫余荣新被抓捕，关押在江门市看守所，谢清约在<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被抓捕，也被关押在江门市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，在未通知律师和家属的情况下，广东江门法院秘密判刑，余荣新被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年半，妻子谢清被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半。谢清刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">谢清玲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">女，山东泰安市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年六十六岁，泰安市化肥厂退休职工。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日上午，谢清玲、高方强等法轮功学员去良庄镇赠送法轮功年历，在回来的路上，警察驾驶围堵抓捕。后泰山区公安分局国保大队与岱庙等派出所撬门破锁，闯入谢清玲家中，将家中所有电脑、打印机、法轮功资料等物品抄走。谢清玲和高方强最后被关押到泰安市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月获悉谢清玲被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，罚款两万元；高方强被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。谢清玲和高方强不服，上诉至泰安市中级法院。泰安中院裁定“维持原判”。后谢清玲转入山东省女子监狱服刑；高方强被转入山东省监狱服刑。谢清玲刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/20/2022-1-20.html#zip5"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/20/2022-1-20.html#zip5</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">谢热扎提<span lang="EN-US">.</span>阿海（哈萨克）</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：<span lang="EN-US">1987</span>年出生，新疆阿尔泰市阿拉哈克乡（<span lang="EN-US">Alagak</span>）人，从事民族特色装修工作者，哈萨克族人权捍卫者、政治犯。因经常频繁与哈萨克斯坦国的亲友联系，遂被当地警方抓捕，并被指控在网上传播暴恐视频等，泄露了国家机密，属于违法行为。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月他被阿尔泰市法院以“泄露国家机密罪”等重判刑期<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。后无任何消息。刑期约至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">谢文飞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">本名谢丰夏。<span lang="EN-US"> 1977</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日出生，湖南省郴州市桂阳县人，网名“谢文飞”、“南街谢文飞”、“南街谢文飞<span lang="EN-US">@njxwf </span>”，人权捍卫者，南方街头运动践行者，政治犯。近年来，因经常活跃于广州街头，勇于为推动中国的民主宪政事业积极发声和献身，故而遭到广东当局的多次打压和拘留；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，曾因前往围观广州公民李伊国申请“六四游行”被拘提起诉讼案开庭，而被广东省佛山市警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，关押于佛山市禅诚区看守所，事由是“纪念林昭和曹顺利”；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，曾因与民主维权公民王福磊、王默等在广州举牌，发起寻找民主异见人士张圣雨的活动，被石围派出所警方带走，且被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，曾因穿着黑衫在广州市街头拉横幅声援香港民主抗争、“真普选”，被广州警方从增城区新塘镇住所再次带走，并以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留；审讯期间，遭酷刑折磨，被广州市越秀看守所警方实施“定镣”处罚，时间长达<span lang="EN-US">104</span>个小时；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，被广州市检察院更换罪名以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”正式批捕，并被转关至广州市第一看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，其案正式开庭受审；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，被广州市中级法院以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，刑满释放。此前在广东省河源监狱服刑。谢文飞于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日晚上在苏仙区租房处被郴州警方强制带走，次日苏仙区公安分局以涉嫌寻衅滋事为由将其刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日其被办案单位苏仙区公安分局移送苏仙区检察院审查起诉，后检察院以谢文飞“涉嫌寻衅滋事”罪向苏仙区法院起诉。谢文飞羁押在郴州市下辖的资兴市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"> 2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日开庭。一直未宣判。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月宣判，谢文飞获刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。后被转监到湖南长沙赤山监狱。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/06/46_25.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/06/46_25.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">谢阳：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1972</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日出生，湖南省长沙市人，天地人律师事务所和长沙京盈科律师事务所前任律师，原湖南纲维律师事务所律师，人权律师，中国在押政治犯。自<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年正式执业以来，曾因代理多起公权力滥权案件，如山东省曲阜县薛明凯案、北京新公民运动张宝成案、河南省南乐县南乐教案、湖南省浏阳市张开华征地案等维权案件，并积极关注和参与社会维权运动（包括探访盲人律师陈光诚和声援建三江被捕律师等），而屡遭司法当局阻扰和逼迫打压；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，曾因只身前往山东省东师古村探望盲人律师陈光陈，而被地方黑恶势力殴打抢劫；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，曾因代理一起民间借贷纠纷案，为维护当事人利益要求取得合议庭商议结果，而被湖南省律师协会罚款<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元，并被所在事务所要求解除合同和离职；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，曾因为“山东薛家命案”作委托代理律师，而被湖南省司法厅当局带走“约谈喝茶”；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，曾因为代理湖南省浏阳市土地维权者张开华案，在出庭时遭到当地法院的野蛮阻扰；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月—<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，因多次代理维权案件，而遭到湖南省律师协会变相打压，不予批准转所手续；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，因其积极代理多起长沙市雨花区强制征地拆迁案件，在代理莲湖村农民征地行政诉讼时，曾遭到当地法院非法驱逐；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，因其代理广西南宁北部湾建材市场当事人的维权案件，曾遭到多名不明身份人员的持械群殴，致其重伤，右腿骨折，其虽报警，但当地警方却迟迟不予出警；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，其在中共“<span lang="EN-US">709</span>大逮捕”中被湖南省长沙市警方抓走，后被以涉嫌“扰乱法庭秩序”、“煽动颠覆国家政权”二罪指定地点监视居住，代理律师要求会见遭拒；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，被长沙市警方以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，其案在湖南省长沙中级法院开庭受审，但因其被迫当庭认罪，否认曾受酷刑，遂于当日暂获取保候审；同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被长沙市中级法院正式宣判：犯煽动颠覆国家政权罪，但免予刑事处罚；后其虽未被判刑入狱，但仍遭长期软禁和贴身监控；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，曾因去岁年末前往湖南省永顺县声援因发表网络言论而被强制关进精神病院的怀孕女教师李田田，遂被长沙市警方带走失联，其住处遭查抄，许多个人物品均被损毁，两台计算机及一个保险柜被搜走；后其家人收到警方通知，知其已于被抓当日，被长沙市警方以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”、“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">谢阳于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被以“涉嫌煽动颠覆国家政权罪”正式逮捕。其</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">代理律师纪中久律师收到长沙市公安局<span lang="EN-US"> 2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日签署的不准予会见的决定书。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，谢阳被控煽动颠覆国家政权罪和寻衅滋事罪被捕。案件目前取保候审被拒、第二次律师会见被拒、扣押的物品归还被拒。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，谢阳辩护人闻宇律师到长沙了解案情，长沙市检察院说，案件还没有到检察院。推测应该是延长了侦查期。然后去看守所，说外地律师一律不让会见。谢阳在看守所的情况，无人知晓。<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">目前谢阳被羁押于长沙市第一看守所（湖南省长沙市长沙县泉塘街道远大二路<span lang="EN-US">1736</span>号，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">410131</span>）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/blog-post_41.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/blog-post_41.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/04/202246.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/04/202246.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">谢志锋：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">安徽省人，基督徒，安徽省芜湖市基督教某家庭教会事工人员，教会学校老师，中国在押良心犯。因信仰基督，并在安徽省芜湖市基督教一家庭教会的教育学堂事工当老师，随遭中共安徽当局在意识形态方面的强力打压；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，被闯入教学点的芜湖市戈江区警方将包括其在内的<span lang="EN-US">10</span>名老师莫名抓走，同时，教学点遭查抄，内中一切物品均被扣押，后其<span lang="EN-US">10</span>人被视为同案嫌疑人统一被芜湖市戈江区警方以涉嫌“非法经营罪”刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月初，除杨志言等<span lang="EN-US">6</span>名老师被准予取保候审外，谢志锋及王明海等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人被芜湖市戈江区检察院以涉嫌“非法经营罪”转正式批捕；据悉，其案已有律师代理。目前被羁押于芜湖市第一看守所（安徽省芜湖市戈江区火龙岗镇白马山村，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">241000</span>）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">谢治群：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">贵州省黔东南苗族侗族自治州（简称黔东南州）凯里市人，基督徒，贵州省凯里市基督复临安息日教会神职人员，教会聚会点传道人，中国在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">20</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">余年前，基督复临安息日教会在贵州省凯里市开始成立聚会点，自此，其一直与教会负责者及多名神职人员通力合作，热忱致力于教会的多种服务工作，尤以带领信徒敬拜和布道为主；但因该教会聚会点长期以来均为家庭教会聚会模式，对中共当局严格把控的“三自教会”管理拒不认同，也不接受（尽管该教会聚会点早已向贵州省宗教局提交请求聚会点合法的申请，但始终莫名未获审批），遂遭贵州当局在意识形态上的严苛限制；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，又因该聚会点信徒不断增多，聚会点已由原先的<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个剧增到<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个，故而很快引起贵州省黔东南州当局的关注与恐慌，并立刻成立项目组，对其聚会点进行全面监控侦查；之后，其及教会长老等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>位神职人员均被黔东南州凯里市警方带走，且被以涉嫌“诈骗罪”刑拘，自此失联；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，谢治群等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人被凯里市检察院以同罪名予以批捕，控其因所属聚会点申请未被国家审批，众信徒所交善款均属于诈骗款，故其在教会里的一切敬拜布道行为均属违法；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，谢治群<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人案在黔东南州凯里市法院统一开庭审理，最终被分别以“诈骗罪”秘密判处<span lang="EN-US">12</span>—<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年不等刑期；其中，谢治群被重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月；另其教会<span lang="EN-US">140</span>万余元奉献款亦被宣判扣押；其不服，提起上诉；但据称，黔东南州中级法院似乎不愿对其上诉案公开审理，且对辩护人提交的新证据也无兴趣；二审正在等待中。目前被羁押于黔东南州凯里市看守所（贵州省<span lang="EN-US">/</span>黔东南苗族侗族自治州<span lang="EN-US">/</span>凯里市<span lang="EN-US">/</span>永乐路，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">556099</span>）。<span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">新杰恩斯汗<span lang="EN-US">. </span>巴格达：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">新疆电视台的哈萨克族配音演员杰恩斯汗<span lang="EN-US">.</span>巴格达因信仰问题也被于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日在乌鲁木齐市的家里被公安人员抓走，至今未归，不知下落。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辛赏<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">男，<span lang="EN-US">1994</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日出生，现年<span lang="EN-US">29</span>岁。因“白纸抗议运动”在北京遭刑事拘留者。曾就读于英国威斯敏斯特大学的纪实摄影专业，回国后从事电影行业。曾于去年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月底参与北京亮马桥抗议，后多次遭警方传唤，最后于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日遭抓捕。辛赏父母已经收到了拘留通知书，拘留书上罪名是危害公共安全罪，目前仍在羁押中。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：山东省临清市法轮功学员，女，家住山东省临清市八岔路乡潘彭店村。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日被当地派出所警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，山东冠县法院对邢爱玲判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚金一万元；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<b mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邢景玉：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北邯郸市法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1948</span>年生，农民，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日因宣传法轮功被抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被大名县公安局刑事拘留，同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日经大名县检察院批准，被执行逮捕。于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被肥乡区检察院以肥向肥乡区法院提起公诉。（侦查阶段在大名县，大名县检察院将邢景玉案卷移送肥乡区检察院）肥乡区法院<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日开庭，邢景玉被肥乡区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">3000</span>元人民币。邢景玉被送唐山市冀东监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源： </span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/09/16.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;
