style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邢望力：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1971</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，河南省信阳市息县人，又名吴全力，维权访民，人权捍卫者，中国在押维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，曾因<span lang="EN-US">7</span>岁幼子邢鉴（时名邢路路）被车祸撞成重伤，地方当局枉法处理且私分赔偿款，自此全家人走上维权道路；因逐级频繁上访，其家数人曾被当局非法拘禁、劳教、判刑等共计达<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年之久，其亦被多次关押拘禁；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，曾因息县维权访民冯国辉在上访期间离奇死于息县农贸市场的出租屋内，邢与妻子等人在网上要求中纪委、公安部等就此事介入彻查，遂惹怒地方当局；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，被息县警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，指控其尿射县法院名称牌子和抗议法院对其女儿邢梅、母亲及岳母的不公判决等；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事”、“敲诈勒索政府”二罪正式逮捕，关押在信阳市息县看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，其案在河南省信阳市息县法院开审，被一审以“ 敲诈勒索政府罪”、“寻衅滋事罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；其不服立即上，不想次日竟险遭死亡，而狱方事发<span lang="EN-US">10</span>小时后才通知家人，称其在监舍窗口试图用裤子上吊自杀，被人救下时，不慎头朝下重撞头部，致其“右侧额颞叶脑挫裂伤、枕骨骨折、左侧顶部硬膜外血肿、两肺下叶挫伤、双侧胸腔积液，脑组织积水”，因未脱离危险期家属不得看望；据悉，其在看守所期间，曾屡遭酷刑折磨和牢狱虐待；后经信阳市中级法院二审裁决，“敲诈勒索政府罪”被取消，最终被以“寻衅滋事罪” 判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日刑满释放后，其夫妇因儿子车祸赔偿款遭时任管理者当局贪污，曾数度被投入狱中，遭到当局强力迫害，夫妻二人疾病缠身，无奈之下于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月底前往北京寻医治病，但从北京火车站下车便被当地政府截访人员绑架、遣返、拘留，之后又被河南省信阳市息县法院以”困难救济<span lang="EN-US">3000</span>人民币”为定罪依据，以“寻衅滋事罪”将其枉判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月；其不服上诉，后经由河南省信阳市中级法院二次密审，依然驳回上诉，维持原判，后送河南省信阳监狱服刑；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，刑满释放；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年，曾因其夫妇二人于<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日前往河南省罗山县灵山镇看望被当局软禁<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年有余的人权律师江天勇，<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，又因在北京市东城区信访投诉，遂再遭北京市前门派出所警员的盘查和拘押，后移交给河南省息县警方，被处行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，行政拘留期满日，又被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”转为刑事拘留；后被批捕。目前被羁押于河南省息县看守所。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2022</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，邢望力的家属首次见到该判决书：河南省信阳市息县法院认定《致社会各界人士及网友的一封求助信》系虚假信息，诽谤多名公职人员，造成社会恶劣影响，将邢望力以“诽谤罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日；其不服，已提起上诉；二审正在对待中。目前被羁押于河南省息县看守所。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/04/211.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/04/211.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">邢文香：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">浙江金华圣爱堂牧师包国华的夫人，于<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被金华市公安局婺城分局以涉嫌非法经营罪、聚众扰乱社会秩序罪、隐匿会计凭证罪、侵占罪四个罪名刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，邢文香被金华市婺城区法院控告犯有“职务侵占罪”、“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”、“非法经营罪”以及“隐匿会计凭证、会计账簿、财务会计报告罪”等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>项罪名，被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年，并处没收财产人民币<span lang="EN-US">60</span>万元，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">9</span>万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">熊成霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江苏省连云港市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，连云港市海州区公安分局抓捕了法轮功学员刘玉萍、邵世玲、那仁志、熊成霞、周翠萍、马宝玲、高建君、王艾芝、汪宝玉、小周女士、乔老太等十一人。所有人家中都被非法抄了家，警察劫走家中的电脑、手机、光盘、<span lang="EN-US">U</span>盘、电器、钱财、书籍等私人物品。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，熊成霞被开庭，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">徐彩虹：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖北维权人士<b>。</b><span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，湖北维权人士何斌、徐彩虹夫妇的家人一大早收到襄阳市樊城区分局的拘留通知书，称何斌、徐彩虹夫妇俩涉嫌寻衅滋事犯罪已被刑事拘留。何斌、徐彩虹夫妇俩是<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日早上被从家中传唤走的，下午家人前去辖区派出所询问，派出所告知人已经被带走了。何斌、徐彩红夫妻因为租赁纠纷案件一直在北京信访，<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被从北京截访人员接回去的，回家后住了一宿再被传唤，<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日家人收到刑事拘留通知书。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/09/blog-post_10.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/09/blog-post_10.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">徐长禄：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁大连市法轮功学员，</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1952</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年生，男，家住大连市长海县广鹿乡沙尖村，因修炼法轮功，曾多次遭中共人员抓捕、关押。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日遭抓捕，后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。徐长禄于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月下旬被转入辽南新入监监狱，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">:2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/24/446728.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/24/446728.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">徐德武：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁抚顺市新宾县苇子峪镇法轮功学员。徐德武<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日上午被当地派出所警察非法带到县公安局，被强行带到抚顺做核酸后，被非法关押在当地看守所，后被抚顺市顺城区检察院非法批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被抚顺市顺城区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">1000</span>元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/4/26/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%9B%9B%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E5%85%AD%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-423853.html#2142523528-1"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/4/26/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%9B%9B%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E5%85%AD%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-423853.html#2142523528-1</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">徐福明：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">与龚圣亮牧师同案。河南省台前县人，基督教华南教会（<span lang="EN-US">SCC</span>）创建人及钟祥交通会骨干成员。曾因其与多人积极参与基督教华南家庭教会创建和发展活动，在成为湖北省荆门市钟祥市教会骨干之后，又力促教会活动发展至湖北、河南、四川等多个省市，使该教会不仅在人数达<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万信徒，而且在实力上也日趋增强，随引起中共强烈不满和极度恐慌，将华南教会定为“邪教”，其亦在此打击“邪教”行动中遭到严重逼迫打压；<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，因被控涉嫌“参与<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月在湖北省钟祥市对受害人谢东报复伤害案”，而被荆门市钟祥市警方以“利用邪教破坏法律实施罪”刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日被正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日被湖北省荆门市中级法院一审以同罪名判处死刑，<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日又经湖北省荆门市中级法院二审，以“故意伤害罪”改判为无期徒刑，剥夺政治权利终身。目前在湖北省某监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">徐光</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：“八九六四”杭州大学学运领袖，中国民主党浙江委员会核心成员。<span lang="EN-US">1968</span>年出生于浙江省富阳市，<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年毕业于杭州大学生物系，大学期间曾参与<span lang="EN-US">1986</span>年及<span lang="EN-US">1989</span>年学生爱国民主运动，<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月在家乡富阳市环保局环境监测站工作的徐光组建了“中国民主党浙江省富阳市筹委会”，是中国民主党第一个县级组织。撰写了《抓不完的中国民主党》等文章，并起草《中国民主党富阳市筹备委员会成立公开宣言》，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被杭州市抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>被逮捕。同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日徐光被以“颠覆国家政权罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年；出狱后的徐光仍坚守信念，抨击时弊。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日因为在<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>上参加中国民主党话题的闲聊，被浙江当局以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被正式逮捕，同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日获释，期间从未获准律师会见。后获释。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日徐光遭当地警方于刑事拘留。罪名为涉嫌寻衅滋事。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日徐光被警方正式逮捕。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2022</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日浙江异议人士徐光家属透露，遭羁押的徐光现在绝食已七十多天，转押在杭州市看守所监管医院。此前律师去杭州市西湖区看守所，未能会见到。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/08/blog-post_87.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/08/blog-post_87.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">徐桂莲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁大连市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年生，家住大连市金州区站前街道龙湾社区民和小区。她是社区工义岗（打扫公共卫生）。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年，徐桂莲开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，遭警方抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，徐桂莲被关押到姚家看守所。此后，大连金州区站前派出所警察和检察院、法院串通，构陷徐桂莲。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月得知，徐桂莲被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，已被劫入位于沈阳于洪区的辽宁省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">江西省南昌市罗家镇法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1951</span>年生，现年<span lang="EN-US">71</span>岁。大学学历，南昌市江南材料厂退休职工，一九九七年一月开始修炼法轮功；后遭中共当局多次迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，南昌市罗家镇徐桂珍等七位法轮功学员在一起学习法轮功著作，被罗家镇派出所警察通过手机定位跟踪，全部被抓捕、抄家。后徐桂珍被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，已被送往江西省女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/6/18/445084.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">徐建鑫：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">上海市法轮功学员</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">。男，出生于<span lang="EN-US">1956</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，今年<span lang="EN-US">68</span>岁，家住上海市闵行区七宝镇，被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月（刑期<span lang="EN-US">:2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日）。现被关押在上海市提篮桥监狱一监区。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/4/458456.html"><b mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吉林永吉县法轮功学员。女，</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">一九七三年四月生。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日下午，在出租车上给司机讲法轮功后被司机诬告，被城南派出所警察抓捕、构陷，关押一年多后送吉林省女子监狱，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月得知她被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/3/2/457322.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">徐衍贞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">山东省胶州法轮功学员，女。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，公安部督办抓捕了胶州徐衍贞等几十个法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，徐衍贞被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">徐强：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁大连市法轮功学员，</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1960</span>年生，家住大连市普兰店区杨树房街道。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，她遭抓捕，后被中共法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个月。于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日被关押到辽宁女子监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">:2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/24/446728.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">徐秦：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，原籍湖北武汉，现居江苏扬州市。民间组织“中国人权观察”（筹）前秘书长，“玫瑰团队”成员，人权活动人士，中国在押政治犯。长期以来，一直关注中国人权状况，并与著名人权活动家、民主异议人士秦永敏一道筹建中国人权观察；自秦永敏被捕、秦之妻子赵素利“被失踪”后，她曾多次上街声援，跟进案件；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，当其准备申请旁听隋牧青律师被吊照听证会时，被警方突然限制自由，之后一直遭跟踪与监控；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，其在从扬州高邮到昆山的途中被警方带走，后得知其被扬州市警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，其家属委托的代理律师要求会见，遭到警方拒绝，但被告知其已于<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日由刑拘转为“指定居所监视居住”；<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，又被追加罪名，以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”继续扣留，且不准律师会见；据悉，此次被捕，皆与其近年来坚持关注人权问题，后又积极组织联署声援维权律师余文生，以及为维权公民徐琳筹款等活动有关；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日获悉，其已获取保释放；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日徐秦被江苏省扬州市中级人民法院指控犯煽动颠覆国家政权罪执行逮捕。现羁押于扬州市看守所。据悉，之前其所涉案件一直处于延审中；又悉，因其刚做完心脏搭桥手术，且患有脑梗、心梗、高血压等多种疾病，故其夫对其身体状况极为担忧。目前被羁押于江苏省扬州市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月获悉，</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">徐秦案再次被江苏省扬州市中级法院延长审理期限<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。这是徐秦案第六次被延期，而批准延期的是最高法院。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，徐秦的代理律师会见到徐秦。徐秦身体情况不太好，血压不稳，视力、听力都有所下降。徐秦表示自己的所作所为是为了社会进步司法进步，关押期间曾三次绝食抗议。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，纪中久律师在扬州看守所会见了徐秦，得知她于<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日瘫痪了。会见时，徐坐在轮椅上，精神疲惫、身体情况很不好。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，在宁夏女子监狱遭受迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，徐润叶结束三年半冤狱，从宁夏女子监狱回家。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日因张贴法轮功真相传单，被银川市公安局金凤区分局长城中路派出所警察抓捕、构陷，近日被银川市西夏区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。目前被关押在银川市看守所<span lang="EN-US">.</span>刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span minor-fareast;">上海维权人士。项文寅、徐玮、李平、俞忠欢、王国财、诸枝花等六人一行，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日去北京的国家信访局正常信访，因国家信访局没有按惯例给予短信回复，怀疑是被违法销号，所以又返回到国家信访局咨询，被北京是公安局月坛派出所拦截后移交上海市驻京办，先扣押身份证后押解回上海关押在长兴岛黑监狱，两天后的<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/07/blog-post_29.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/07/blog-post_29.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormalCxSpMiddle" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-add-space: auto; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">徐孝兰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">山东省高密市法轮功学员。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">2021</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月份，徐孝兰被当地派出所诱骗，说是到所里来一趟，然后被拉到高密市检察院签字，其实签的是批捕的条子。从此，徐孝兰再也没有回家。现在在哪家人和朋友都不知道。经多方打听，徐孝兰被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，高密市公检法暗箱操作，没有任何消息通知家人，偷偷地判了。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/6/7/2022-6-7.html#2266222931-1"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/6/7/2022-6-7.html#2266222931-1</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">徐秀娟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">法轮功学员徐秀娟，家在秦皇岛市北港镇，女，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年五十来岁，因为信仰法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，被中共警察抓捕，关押在秦皇岛市第一看守所。被抓捕后，现在在公安医院监护中，徐秀娟的身体处于危险状态，高血压、贫血、心衰，血压最高达到二百四十。亲朋好友一直在找看守所和法院交涉。但是他们互相推诿，拿法轮功学员的生命当儿戏。徐秀娟于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日被庭审，遭海港区法院、秦皇岛中级法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，被关押到河北石家庄女子监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">徐颜华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1952</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日出生，退休职工，家住吉林省磐石市红旗岭镇。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年开始修炼法轮功。自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年中共当局开始疯狂迫害法轮功后，徐颜华与家人屡遭中共迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，徐颜华的儿子王鹏家遭抓捕。随后，王鹏被刑事拘留，关押在长春市公安监管中心（苇子沟看守所）。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，王鹏被宽城区法院以疫情为由到看守所开庭。后王鹏被判<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。徐颜华是于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被长春市净月区彩宇大街派出所警察抓捕的，后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/09/5.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/09/5.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/9/9/%E4%B8%8E%E5%AE%B6%E4%BA%BA%E5%B1%A1%E9%81%AD%E4%B8%AD%E5%85%B1%E8%BF%AB%E5%AE%B3-%E9%95%BF%E6%98%A5%E5%B8%82%E5%BE%90%E9%A2%9C%E5%8D%8E%E5%8F%88%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%BA%94%E5%B9%B4-465122.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/9/9/%E4%B8%8E%E5%AE%B6%E4%BA%BA%E5%B1%A1%E9%81%AD%E4%B8%AD%E5%85%B1%E8%BF%AB%E5%AE%B3-%E9%95%BF%E6%98%A5%E5%B8%82%E5%BE%90%E9%A2%9C%E5%8D%8E%E5%8F%88%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%BA%94%E5%B9%B4-465122.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">徐英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江省牡丹江海林市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1969</span>年生，原牡丹江海林市子荣小学教师。因修炼法轮功曾屡遭迫害。徐英于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日被海林市公安局国保大队抓捕，当日被劫持到牡丹江看守所关押迫害。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，她被海林市法院秘密庭审。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月获悉：她被海林市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年。<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/12/15/453135.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/12/15/453135.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">徐永清：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1964</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年出生，浙江省龙泉市人，上海市静安区延安西路居民，上海市楼宇建筑弱电专家，上海建瓯信息科技有限公司高级工程师，法轮功信仰者，中国在押良心犯。因其个性为人真诚，乐于助人，办事认真且精通业务，故而在任职公司中深受众人好评与尊重，但却因信仰法轮功遭到中共上海当局的严打和监控；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，曾因上海市漕宝路地铁站出现有诬蔑法轮功的画板，出于对自由信仰的维护，其与他人共同向上海市人民大道<span lang="EN-US">200</span>号市政府信访办予以反映，请求撤掉画板，但此举随即遭到上海当局强烈不满和忌恨，并以当时<span lang="EN-US">G20</span>峰会即将召开，“信访时间不合适”为由，将其迅速抓捕并抄家；获释后，因其就<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日中共中央、国务院和公安部联合发布的《公安部关于认定和取缔邪教组织若干问题的通知》（以下简称“取缔”）中罗列的<span lang="EN-US">14</span>种邪教组织名单没有法轮功，也即表明公安部不认为法轮功是邪教，故而针此，其遂于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月向公安部提出“信息公开”申请，并请求公安部对“取缔”一文是否被作废，如若作废，其作废时间和审批程序等予以答复；因公安部一直未给予作答，其遂于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月以公安部“行政不作为”又向北京市中级法院提出起诉；而此举再次招致中共当局更严厉的打击和报复。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，上海警方以“商谈行政复议”为由将其诱骗至上海市大统路<span lang="EN-US">199</span>号面谈，作完笔录后随即将其以涉嫌“宣传法轮功光盘”为罪由刑拘于海市闸北区看守所；后其虽被释放，但<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，其又被扬州市邗江区警方以“从邮局截获<span lang="EN-US">13</span>封法轮功真相信件”为由从家中抓捕刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，被地方检察院以涉嫌“邪教罪”正式批捕，并被关押在扬州市看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，被江苏省扬州市邗江区法院一审以“邪教罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元；其不服上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，扬州市中级法院经二审裁决，依然维持原判，后送江苏省洪泽湖监狱服刑；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，刑满释放；据悉，其在羁押审讯期间，曾遭酷刑虐待，后在监狱服刑时又被奴役，并遭三次暴力殴打，致身心遭严重受损，会见时几乎站立不住；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，当其从老家浙江省龙泉市返回上海的途中，在龙泉火车站被警方再次拘捕；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，其案被浙江省丽水市莲都区法院开庭审理，同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，被该法院一审以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”枉判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，并处罚金一万元，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月；其不服，已当庭表示上诉；至今二审等待中。目前被羁押于丽水市看守所（浙江省丽水市路湾隧道边，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">323700</span>）。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/4_27.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/4_27.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 122.5pt; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">许朝晖：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河南南阳法轮功学员。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">8</span>点，河南方城县公安局伙抓捕了许朝晖，并抄家。<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">许朝晖</span>被关押<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天后，转到南阳看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，许朝晖被唐河县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/4/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%81%E4%BA%8C%E6%9C%88%E5%9B%9B%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-434367.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/4/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%81%E4%BA%8C%E6%9C%88%E5%9B%9B%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-434367.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">许方泉：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东济南市法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">1968</span>年生，济南钢铁集团（简称济钢，原为济南钢铁厂）管理技术人员，大学毕业，家住山东省济南市。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，许方泉去江苏连云港市女儿家探亲，他给路人赠送法轮功好的册子，被人举报，警察通过监控抓捕了许方泉。现被关押在连云港看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，江苏省连云港市海州区法院对许方泉开庭审理。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，许方泉被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 122.5pt; text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://big5.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/8/25/%E5%B1%B1%E6%9D%B1%E7%9C%81%E6%BF%9F%E5%8D%97%E5%B8%82%E8%A8%B1%E6%96%B9%E6%B3%89%E5%9C%A8%E6%B1%9F%E8%98%87%E7%9C%81%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E5%85%A9%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-464546.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://big5.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/8/25/%E5%B1%B1%E6%9D%B1%E7%9C%81%E6%BF%9F%E5%8D%97%E5%B8%82%E8%A8%B1%E6%96%B9%E6%B3%89%E5%9C%A8%E6%B1%9F%E8%98%87%E7%9C%81%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E5%85%A9%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-464546.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">许凤梅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河南周口市东新区法轮功女学员，<span lang="EN-US">1950</span>年代生人。家住周口市东新区许湾乡许湾村。曾于<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年遭劳教迫害<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月被警察入室抓捕、抢劫，关押到周口看守所。接着，邪党公、检、法人员又构陷罪名，将其判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">许高瑞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖北孝感市孝南区新铺镇政府法轮功学员许章清涂爱莲之子。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日晚许章清、涂爱莲夫妇、许章清的儿子许高瑞遭警方抓捕，后遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。湖北孝感市下辖安陆市法院<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日下达对许章清<span lang="EN-US">1</span>家<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人的判决：许章清被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，妻子涂爱莲被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，他们未修炼法轮功的儿子许高瑞被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；同时每人还被勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。许高瑞刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">许丽华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">吉林省榆树市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1948</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年七十三岁。二零一一年，许丽华曾被判刑三年，一直在吉林省女子监狱遭迫害三年。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">许丽华在<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月疫情期间，在大街上贴法轮功传单，被人诬陷，遭华昌派出所警察抓捕、后“取保候审”。华昌派出所警察仍在继续构陷许丽华老太至德惠市检察院和法院。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，许丽华老太被德惠市法院判刑三年，已被押入吉林省女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/20/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-437033.html</span></u></b><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">许那（又名许娜）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，当年天安门广场上的绝食学生中，有一位名叫许那（又名许娜），是北京广播学院（现中国传媒大学）的学生。<span lang="EN-US">32</span>年前，她曾和同学高举“新闻自由，言论自由”的横幅，满怀希望地走在北京街头游行的人群中。<span lang="EN-US">32</span>年后，许那仍在北京，却已在东城区看守所被刑事羁押了一年多时间。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，许那和于宙在参加一场同道聚会后双双被拘留四十多天。<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，许那因为外地来京的法轮功朋友提供住宿而再次被捕，后被判五年有期徒刑。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年初，随着奥运会的临近，各地异议人士遭到抓捕，包括法轮功修炼者。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日晚上，于宙、许那在演唱会结束后开车回家的路上，被警方拦住搜查。警察在其车中搜出一本法轮功书籍，将夫妇二人带到通州拘留所。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>天后正值除夕，体格健壮的于宙突然离奇死亡，时年<span lang="EN-US">42</span>岁。当局声称于宙死于绝食或糖尿病。悲痛欲绝的许那被判处三年有期徒刑。于宙的真实死因至今成谜。于宙、许那的案件见于国际特赦<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月向联合国普遍定期审议递交的报告、美国“国会及行政当局中国委员会”的分析报告、美国国际宗教自由委员会<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年度报告。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，许那第三次被捕。当天<span lang="EN-US">13</span>名法轮功修炼者被北京警方抓捕，包括许那在内的<span lang="EN-US">11</span>位被指控“破坏法律实施罪”。许那等人被逮捕起诉涉及在疫情期间发布一些国内疫情照片及与其法轮功修炼者的身份有关。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，许那被北京当局宣判，获刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/8.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/8.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">许晓琴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">重庆市永川区法轮功学员，女，许晓琴于<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年开始修炼法轮大法。中共迫害法轮功后，许晓琴坚持信仰，多次遭中共迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月被警察抓捕后，一直被关押在重庆市永川看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月初，许晓琴已被当地公检法判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。许晓琴已上诉。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月。信<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">息来源：<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"> </span></b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/5/9/459933.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/5/9/459933.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">许秀云：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1959</span>年生，辽宁抚顺市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，许秀云到李石寨发法轮功真相资料，被警察抓捕，许秀云被关入戒毒所。<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，许秀云被判刑<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，许秀云被关押到辽宁女子监狱，遭受惨无人道的酷刑折磨：<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，刑满出狱。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日下午两点左右，许秀云在西一路交通岗附近给路人免费发送翻墙卡，被两个便衣抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，被抚顺市东洲法院开庭，法官田浩以许秀云曾冤狱十三年、出狱未出五年为借口，诬陷其「累犯」，再重判<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">许艳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1982</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日出生，天津市人，北京市石景山区八角北路<span lang="EN-US">24</span>楼租住居民，人权律师余文生之妻，基督徒，推特账号<span lang="EN-US">l@xuyan709</span>，<span lang="EN-US"> 709</span>维权系列案家属之一，人权捍卫者，中国在押政治犯。自从与人权律师余文生结婚以后，夫妻感情甚笃，且一直支持丈夫对自由民主及人权理念的追求；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年，曾为丈夫因涉嫌香港占中运动被中共当局抓捕而维权；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年，曾因丈夫发表《修宪公民建议书》，提出删除“宪法序言”等政治改革建议，而被北京市石景山警方以涉嫌“妨害公务罪”刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年被江苏省徐州市中级法院以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，直至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年才刑满获释，遂其为寻求正义而为丈夫身陷囹圄不断呼吁和维权；然而因其为夫维权发声被中共当局视为需要监控和打压的维稳对象，故而频遭当局骚扰和虐待；后在众多维权律师、正义人士及维权公民的鼎力支持、帮助下，以及在德国驻华大使馆官员和欧盟驻中国代表团等的关注、呼吁下，最终度过其人生中最艰困的时刻，并与被囚<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年刑满出狱的丈夫得以团聚；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，因其夫妇二人受邀参加欧盟驻华代表团座谈会见，遂在前往会见的途中被北京市石景山八角派出所警方拦截传唤，后即失联；<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，其夫妇均被石景山区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，家遭查抄；同年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，其二人又被以同罪名转正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，其代理律师到看守所要求与其会见遭到拒绝，随后被告知其涉罪又被新增“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”。目前被羁押于北京市石景山区看守所（北京市石景山区古城南里甲<span lang="EN-US">1</span>号， 邮政编号：<span lang="EN-US">100043</span>）。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/06/blog-post_11.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/06/blog-post_11.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">许章清：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖北孝感市孝南区新铺镇政府公务员，法轮功学员。每天早出晚归，工作兢兢业业几十年。妻子涂爱莲，是孝南区新铺镇远大小学退休教师，退休才<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多，在家帮忙带孙女。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日晚许章清、涂爱莲夫妇、许章清的儿子许高瑞遭警方抓捕，后遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。湖北孝感市下辖安陆市法院<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日下达对许章清<span lang="EN-US">1</span>家<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人的判决：许章清被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，妻子涂爱莲被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，他们未修炼法轮功的儿子许高瑞被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；同时每人还被勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。许章清刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">许志永：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1973</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日出生，河南省商丘市民权县人，前北京邮电学院专业讲师，前北京市海淀区人民法院人民陪审员，“公盟”重要创始人，青年法学家、宪政学者和公民维权代理人，就全国人大对《城市流浪乞讨人员收容遣送办法》进行违宪审查提议者，新公民运动倡导者，民主公民，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，曾被当选为北京市海淀区第<span lang="EN-US">13</span>届人大代表，同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，曾于与滕彪、俞江和张星水共创民间公益组织“阳光宪道社会科学研究中心”（简称“阳光宪政”）；<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年，曾与范亚峰、滕彪、秋风、王怡等法律学者共同起草《完善我国宪法人权保护条款的建议》；<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年，曾因“阳光宪政”无法继续在北京民政局注册而更名为“北京公盟咨询有限责任公司”（简称“公盟”）；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，曾积极参与推动北京律协的民主选举，同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，又与他人共同草拟、发布《顺应历史潮流，实现律协直选——致全体北京律师、市司法局、市律协的呼吁》和《北京律师协会选举程序（草案）》，引发各界广泛关注，同时也引起中共当局强烈不满和恐慌；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，“公盟”被当局取缔，同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，其亦被北京警方以“偷税罪”逮捕，后又被取保候审；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，“公盟”再次更名为“公民”，继续从事公益维权活动，开始以推动“自由•公义•爱”为主旨的新公民运动。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，其被北京警方再次传唤；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，其海淀区法院人民陪审员职务被北京市海淀区第<span lang="EN-US">15</span>届人民代表大会常务委员会免除；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，被北京市警方以涉嫌“聚扰乱公共场所秩序罪”刑拘，关押在北京市第三看守所；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被北京市第一中级法院以“聚众扰乱公共场所秩序罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，二审维持原判，并送北京柳林监狱（又称天津市汉沽区柳林监狱）服刑；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，刑满释放；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，因在厦门市组织了一次公民运动人士聚会，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月初，又因就<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年新冠肺炎疫情问题发表有关呼吁中共最高领导人习近平“让位”的《劝退书》，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，遂被广州市警方从番禺海鸥岛杨斌律师处抓走，并被以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，又被山东省烟台市警方以同罪名转正式逮捕，并称其与丁家喜并案处理；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，终被山东省临沂市中级法院以“颠覆国家政权罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2034</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月。目前被羁押于烟台市临沭县看守所。</span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> </span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/04/14.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/04/14.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">薛爱梅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">广东</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">深圳市南山区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月出生，，会计，家住深圳市南山区桃源街道水木丹华小区。她善良敦厚、学习优异，她原在美国南伊利诺大学读经济学研究生，<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年，回国探亲时，她派发法轮功真相资料时，遭绑架，<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，被劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，从此再也没能返回美国完成学业。<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年，薛爱梅再被劳教<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，她被福田区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，在广东省女子监狱服刑。她人生最好的年华，都在中共的囚牢中度过。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，薛爱梅乘坐八十一路公交车外出时，发放法轮功资料被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年初，被南山区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金五千元。她上诉后，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，深圳市中级法院维持原判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/6/23/%E6%9B%BE%E9%81%AD%E4%B9%9D%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A%E5%9B%B9%E5%9C%84-%E6%B7%B1%E5%9C%B3%E8%96%9B%E7%88%B1%E6%A2%85%E5%86%8D%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-445298.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">薛桂云</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：吉林桦甸法轮功学员，住桦甸市夹皮沟小区，女，<span lang="EN-US">1969</span>年生。因为修炼法轮功，薛桂云<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日遭抓捕、劳教一年，在黑嘴子女子劳教所遭受迫害；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日又被抓捕，被秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，在黑嘴子女子监狱遭受各种酷刑、体罚折磨、精神虐待<span lang="EN-US">.</span>桦甸市夹皮沟小区薛桂云和布玉新<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日晚在街里贴法轮功资料，被桦甸市明华派出所巡警抓捕。随后，警察抄了两人的家。后被关押在吉林市看守所。布玉新、薛桂云<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被开庭，布玉新被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，薛桂云被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。薛桂云刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">薛丽威：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江大庆市林甸县法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1974</span>年生，大专文化，林甸县第二中学数学教师。<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年开始炼法轮功。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，由黑龙江省公安厅“督办”，大庆市公安局和林甸县公安局出动五十多个便衣警察，暴力抓捕了大庆市林甸县法轮功学员薛丽威、王玉红、路朝波、董娜、陈卫波等。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，大庆让胡路区法院枉法判决：路朝波、王玉红被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年、罚款七万元。薛丽威、陈卫波被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、罚款四万元，董娜被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、罚款三万元。关押在黑龙江省女子监狱。薛丽威刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/12/30/454021.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/12/30/454021.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">薛莲霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东省青岛市黄岛区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，黄岛区西海岸（原胶南）薛莲霞在大珠山某小区发真相资料时，被一青年人恶意举报。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，薛莲霞被黄岛区大珠山派出所抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日上午，薛莲霞被取保候审，女儿去派出所交了<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元保证金。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日下午，薛连霞被胁迫去了法院就没回来。她家人听人说，她被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">薛少强：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">安徽蚌埠活石归正教会长老。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，蚌埠活石归正教会的牧师万长春被安徽省蚌埠市公安局禹会分局以“涉嫌非法经营罪<span lang="EN-US">"</span>刑事拘留。随后，薛少强长老、万春琴同工，还有另外一个基督徒也以相同的罪名先后被刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，又被更改罪名，蚌埠经禹会区人民检察院批准，蚌埠禹会分局以“诈骗罪”对他们批捕。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/08/4.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/08/4.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">薛玉春：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">山东省青岛市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1960</span>年生。家住青岛市黄岛区长江路街道办事处张宝湾社区。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，中共开始发动迫害法轮功，从那时至今，薛玉春至少被中共人员抓捕十次、拘留<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次、骚扰不计其数；<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，她被劫持到山东省淄博市王村劳教所劳教两年。她曾遭受残暴酷刑，在<span lang="EN-US">20</span>年前被劳教所折磨致精神失常。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，薛玉春在长江路的多元批发市场给民众讲法轮功真相时，被长江路派出所警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月被黄岛区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span minor-fareast;">宇美霞、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">袁华秀、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">袁王柱、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">袁志强、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">岳春光、岳乃亮、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">牙里坤<span lang="EN-US">.</span>肉孜（维吾尔）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">新疆维吾尔自治区人，维吾尔名<span lang="EN-US">YalqunRozi</span>，维吾尔族知名作家、讲师和学者，原新疆教育出版社高级编辑，中国在押政治犯。作为高级知识分子，因其长期花费精力编辑了一大批维吾尔人文教科书，发表过若干有关维吾尔文化文章，并于<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年帮助编写了中小学校维吾尔教学大纲和语文教学课程，随颇受社会广泛欢迎，并成为维吾尔知识分子中的典范；但自<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月陈全国被任命为新疆党委书记起，因其极左思想将从事维吾尔教科书的工作均视为“意识形态问题的表现”，故而其及众多同行遂遭严酷打压；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，其及其所属教科书编辑公司的全体成员突遭乌鲁木齐市警方抓捕，因抓捕之初并未受到指控，故其涉嫌罪名不详，但自此失联；据悉，因其自被捕至判刑以来，一直无具体信息，故而其身体健康状况及所押地点等均不知情；其家属请求探视、通信权等亦遭拒绝。目前服刑监狱缺详。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年，知其被中共新疆当局以“颠覆国家政权罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2031</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">闫护救：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">甘肃省天水市</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，闫护救正在自家门市部经营农资生意，突遭中共人员入室抓捕。一年多来，他不放弃信仰，家人被看守所拒绝会见。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月得知，他遭中共秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/12/2/452607.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; 0pt;">吉林</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">长春法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年生。家住长春市二道区吉盛小区。一九九八年修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被二道区东盛派出所入室抓捕，原因是“取保候审”到期，她被检察院起诉，被关押到看守所。家属请律师的手续还没办完，朝阳区法院就急切地暗箱操作，判她<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span 0pt;">辽宁锦州凌海法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日生，今年<span lang="EN-US">52</span>岁，家住辽宁省凌海市建业乡新安村。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，法轮功学员闫琳女士被盐城市公安局盐都区分局政保支队抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月下旬，被大丰区法院判刑<span mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">闫淑芳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林省通化市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年生。闫淑芳于<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年开始修炼法轮大法。因她坚持真、善、忍信仰，多次被中共人员抓捕、关押，在派出所、看守所、洗脑班、劳教所、监狱遭受迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被通化市东昌区公安分局国保大队警察抓捕，关押在通化市看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月初被柳河县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/5/24/461197.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">闫卫宾：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年出生，河南省驻马店市人，原驻马店市政府直属宾馆经理，维权上访者，法轮功学员，中国在押良心犯。自<span lang="EN-US">1995</span>年起，曾因身患乙肝而开始锻炼法轮功，一年后身体复查竟然显示肝功能指标已经正常，故此笃信法轮功；然而，因其追求的宗教信仰与中共政府所宣传的意识形态相左，遂自此屡遭中共公检法部门监控、野蛮抓捕、拘押及劳教等严酷打压；<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，曾因法轮功始遭中共政府迫害，其与家人一同进京请愿和向当局申明法轮功不是邪教，故而被河南警方统一抓捕；<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，曾因再次进京和平请愿并在天安门打横幅抗议，而被北京警方抓捕，后被以“邪教罪”处劳动教养<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，送北京市团河劳教所（现已更名为北京市监狱团河二监区）关押；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，曾因对他人宣讲法轮功的真相及功用，而被驻马店市驿城区雪松派出所警方行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，因给路人发放法轮功宣传单张，被人举报，遂再被驻马店市驿城区老街派出所警方野蛮抄家、抓走，后被以涉嫌邪教罪名刑拘，并被关押在驻马店市看守所；同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，其被驻马店市驿城区检察院以同罪名予以批捕，并称其案因是中央“清零行动”直接定下的“政治案”，属河南省“大案要案”，因而必要“重判”；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，其案被检察院移交到驻马店市驿城区法院；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日<span lang="EN-US">-12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，其案在驿城区法院两次秘审，终被一审以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年；其不服，上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年，经河南省驻马店市中级法院二审裁决，依然维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。目前在河南省新乡女子监狱（河南省新乡市化工路与劳动南路交叉口向南一公里，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">453000</span>）服刑。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/7_22.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/7_22.html</span></b></a></span><b><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">闫文成：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东省沂水县法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1956</span>年生，家住沂水县沂城街道武家洼社区。自中共<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月发动迫害法轮功后，闫文成及其家人多次遭中共的抓捕、抄家、勒索、劳教等迫害；闫文成曾两次被劳教，他二女儿在未成年时就遭劳教，他的老母亲经不起中共人员连续几年的恐吓于<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年含冤去世。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，闫文成被沂水县城北派出所警察抓捕、抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日他被沂水县判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/8/3/%E6%9B%BE%E4%B8%A4%E6%AC%A1%E9%81%AD%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%8A%B3%E6%95%99-%E5%B1%B1%E4%B8%9C%E6%B2%82%E6%B0%B4%E5%8E%BF%E9%97%AB%E6%96%87%E6%88%90%E9%81%AD%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4-463753.html"><b mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font:
