minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">姚淑霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黑龙江海林市法轮功学员，女。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，海林市老年法轮功学员姚淑霞失联，家人发现家中的大法书籍也不见了。经家人四处打听，一天以后，得知姚淑霞被海林第四派出所抓捕，被拘禁在海林拘留所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被海林市法院开庭，她自辩无罪。仅八天后，法官告诉姚淑霞的家人，姚淑霞已被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，有十天的上诉期。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">姚小艳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">宁夏银川市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1981</span>年生。姚小艳<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日在家门口被银川市永宁县公安局警察抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日被刑事拘留；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被银川市西夏区检察院批准逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，西夏区法院对姚小艳庭审，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，勒索罚金二万元。后上诉被驳回。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/2/18/456889.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/2/18/456889.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">姚中群：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">重庆市北碚区法轮功学员。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">2021</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日姚中群被重庆市北碚区国保警察抓捕<span lang="EN-US">,2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被法院开庭判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/24/446659.html#22723233435-1"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/24/446659.html#22723233435-1</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">叶尔江•胡阿西：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">新疆伊犁州巩留县人，哈萨克族公民，穆斯林，伊犁州巩留县吉尔格郎乡阿勒玛勒村清真寺伊玛目（即穆斯林集体礼拜时的领祷人或清真寺的教长等领袖人物），中国在押良心犯。自<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年起，因中共政府对新疆地区各少数族裔施行更严酷的高压管控政策，遂中共新疆当局开始大规模抓捕维吾尔族、哈萨克斯坦族穆斯林，清除所有带有少数民族文化特征的标志、广告牌、清真食品，甚至收缴或焚烧《古兰经》，并将数以万计的穆斯林强行送入所谓的“职业技能教育培训中心”（又叫新疆再教育营，休息介绍见面）；接受汉化教育等。对于少数民族聚会，更是设法取缔；后在国际社会关注下，从<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年初开始，中共当局被迫将一部分在押培训者予以释放，但于此同时，又将另一部分人予以重判入狱；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，其因与所在村落清真寺里的穆斯林共同欢庆每年一度的纳乌鲁斯节（突厥民族的传统节日）时，做了穆斯林特有的敬拜仪式，随后即被伊犁州巩留县吉尔格郎乡警方抓走，同期另有<span lang="EN-US">5</span>名清真寺穆斯林亦被抓走，并被悉数送进当地一所“再教育营”接受洗脑培训和关押，自此失联；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年获悉，其等一行<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人已被伊犁州巩留县警方以涉嫌“非法集会，传扬不正当的宗教等”罪名予以拘捕，并被伊犁州巩留县检察院起诉至巩留县法院；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-3</span>月，其等<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人案在伊犁州巩留县法院被以“非法集会罪”和“非法传播宗教罪”分别密判<span lang="EN-US">18</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-21</span>年不等刑期，其中，叶尔江•胡阿西被重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">21</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2039</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。目前在新疆新源监狱（新疆伊犁州新源县喀拉布拉镇，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">835813</span>）服刑。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/09/21.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/09/21.html</span></b></a></span><b><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">叶尔灭克﹒木思林：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1980</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日出生，新疆昌吉回族自治州木垒县人，回族，木垒县东城镇鸡心梁村村民。因在微信群发出了向往哈萨克斯坦国并希望前往该国等信息，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被木垒县县公安局刑事拘留，自此杳无音讯。据悉，被抓之前，他一无护照，二也从未出境到过哈萨克斯坦国，仅作为一位普通村民，在微信朋友群里发了个帖子，说说个人的想法，并未发表批评政府的言论。其家人说，当地公安以检查为由，先是拿走他的手机，几天后又把他抓走，此后再不知下落，也不准家人见面。截至目前，其一直在押未放。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">耶尔肯别克•达列力（哈萨克）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">他与玛乌提•么斯尔汗（哈萨克）<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">、</b></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">纳杂尔﹒叶尔江、哈纳提别克﹒萨布尔别克、阿尔恒﹒巴杂尔别克、乌木别提﹒卡斯木、哈伊拉提别克﹒木合塔尔汗、沙部旦﹒沙伊合、耶尔肯别克﹒达列力、肯杰别克﹒达列力都是新疆伊利市哈萨克自治州阿尔泰市巴里巴盖乡人，哈萨克族，穆斯林。其中，纳杂尔﹒叶尔江<span lang="EN-US">26</span>岁，哈纳提别克﹒萨布尔别克<span lang="EN-US">26</span>岁，阿尔恒﹒巴杂尔别克<span lang="EN-US">27</span>岁，乌木别提﹒卡斯木<span lang="EN-US">31</span>岁，哈伊拉提别克﹒木合塔尔汗<span lang="EN-US">37</span>岁，沙部旦﹒沙伊合约<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁，<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">耶尔肯别克﹒达列力<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁，</b>肯杰别克﹒达列力<span lang="EN-US">27</span>岁，玛乌提﹒么斯尔汗约<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-8</span>月，因他们分别在私下里进行了穆斯林传统常规祷告仪式，而被中共新疆伊犁市哈萨克自治州阿尔泰当局知晓后拘捕，遂很快被阿尔泰市地方法院以“非法从事宗教活动”和“从事宗教极端活动”为由分别判处<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-6</span>年不等刑期。目前各人具体判刑不详，刑至日期不详，服刑监狱不详，服刑状况及健康程度等不详。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">伊力哈木•土赫提（维吾尔）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1969</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日出生，新疆维吾尔自治区阿图什人，原中央民族大学维吾尔族教师，维族学者，维汉双语网站“维吾尔在线”创建人。曾于<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年创办维吾尔在线网站，<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年新疆乌鲁木齐发生“<span lang="EN-US">7</span>•<span lang="EN-US">5</span>”事件期间，因该网站被当局视为进行了“大肆煽动宣传，传播谣言”的活动，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，伊力哈木及其家人即被中共当局带走，隔离软禁于北京周边某处，后来在作家王力雄等数百人联署的《关于维吾尔学者伊力哈木•土赫提遭拘押的呼吁》之下，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，才被释放回家；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，又因北京发生天安门撞桥事件，遂于<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日在开车带孩子及妻子外出时遭遇国保便衣警察的驾车冲撞及恐吓。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，再次被北京及新疆警察从家中带走刑拘，被羁押于新疆自治区公安厅看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，被乌鲁木齐市人民检察院以涉嫌“分裂国家罪”正式批捕，理由是“伊力哈木•土赫提与境外‘东突’势力勾结”，利用互联网鼓吹‘新疆独立’，利用讲堂煽动<span lang="EN-US">'</span>推翻政府<span lang="EN-US">'</span>，利用教师身份从事分裂活动”；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，最终被新疆自治区中级法院以“分裂国家罪”重判无期徒刑，没收个人全部财产；其不服上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日经二审依然维持原判。目前在新疆自治区第一监狱服刑。其亲属前往探视，送钱及衣服等物品遭狱方拒绝，理由竟是伊力哈木的钱尚未用完，被羁押者无需送衣物。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">伊克帕·阿萨特（维吾尔族）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1986</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年出生，新疆维吾尔族自治区乌鲁木齐市人，维吾尔族名<span lang="EN-US">Ekpar Asat</span>，新疆维吾尔族某社群媒体创办人，知名维吾尔族创业家，中国政府眼中的“模范维吾尔公民”，中国在押政治犯。因被中共官方誉为“模范维吾尔公民”，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年，曾多次受邀参加新疆当局举办的各种社会活动，包括曾与新疆政府合办过一场中国与中亚各国之间的拳击比赛等，不仅受到新疆当地民众广泛赞誉，更被中共新疆当局称为能“带来正面影响的人”；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，曾因应邀参加一个由美国国务院举办的有关领导力培训项目，时间为期三周，并在中国代表团中是唯一的少数民族参与者，又因培训期间会见了同在美国哈佛大学完成法学硕士课程的姐姐莱汉·阿萨特（现已是维吾尔族律师，居住在美国首都华盛顿特区），遂在回国三周后，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月初，突然被失踪，后知被中共新疆乌鲁木齐市警方以涉嫌“极端份子为罪由”刑拘和逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，从中国驻美大使馆回复美国议员库恩斯<span lang="EN-US">(Chris Coons)</span>的电邮中得知，其已被新疆乌鲁木齐市法院以“煽动民族仇恨罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2031</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月。目前在新疆自治区乌鲁木齐市某监狱（疑似在新疆第一监狱）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">伊敏江•拉赫米图拉（维吾尔）</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：<span lang="EN-US">1962</span>年出生，新疆维吾尔自治区<span lang="EN-US">/</span>克孜勒苏柯尔克孜自治州<span lang="EN-US">/</span>阿图什市人，维吾尔族，新疆福江果业集团有限公司、新疆布格拉农产品开发有限公司、布格拉房地产有限公司、布格拉购物中心和新疆喀什大巴扎（维吾尔族语，即集贸市场）等公司创始人、负责者，维吾尔族亿万富豪之<span lang="EN-US">1</span>，知名慈善企业家，中国在押政治犯。早年，曾就读于新疆金融大学（现更名为新疆财经大学金融学院），毕业后，最初在政府部门供职，数年后开始转而从事商业活动；曾投资<span lang="EN-US"> 5000 </span>万元人民币（合<span lang="EN-US">780</span>万美元）成立了新疆福江果业集团有限公司，后又陆续创立了新疆布格拉农产品开发有限公司、布格拉房地产有限公司、布格拉购物中心（<span lang="EN-US">Bughra Commercial Market</span>）及新疆喀什大巴扎等共计<span lang="EN-US">9</span>大公司，不仅丰富了当地维吾尔小区居民的生活供应，而且为当地维吾尔人创造了显着的就业机会，为阿图什等市的贫困人口提供了大量救助资金；此外，还在将新疆南部的农产品及其他产品引入中亚市场方面发挥了主导作用，故而深受新疆政府的极大赞许和肯定；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，其突然被新疆阿图什市警方以涉嫌“支持恐怖分子”罪名刑拘，其女儿及其姐妹努尔古丽•拉赫米图拉<span lang="EN-US"> (Nurgul Rahmitulla) </span>亦被拘留；之后其又被阿图什市检察院以同罪名转正式逮捕，指控其在“为个人财产缴纳天课”（即从事慈善事业）时向被囚的维吾尔族政治犯的家属捐款，此行为触犯了政府相关政策和法律法规；后经两年的调查，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年初，终被新疆阿图什中级法院以“支持恐怖分子”和“为恐怖主义准备”罪重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">20</span>年；其不服，上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，经克孜勒苏柯尔克孜自治州中级法院<span lang="EN-US">2</span>审裁决：驳回上诉，维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2038</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月；据悉，被押初期，曾遭酷刑折磨，并在酷刑胁迫下被迫承认了一些“罪行”，以换取其女被释放，但最终其女仍然被判入狱。目前疑似在阿克苏监狱或沙雅监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/12/20_20.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/12/20_20.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">依司马伊利<span lang="EN-US">. </span>斯迪克（维吾尔族）： </span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">维吾尔族农民。<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日生，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被羁押，仅仅<span lang="EN-US">5</span>天后，就被新疆英吉沙县法院以宣扬极端主义罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，判刑如此神速，说明他此前很可能已被关在维吾尔人集中营。依司马伊利<span lang="EN-US">. </span>斯迪克被转送监狱半年后，他被同囚的维吾尔人举报在监狱做礼拜，他很生气就骂维吾尔人不团结，结果他又被新疆建设兵团法院以煽动民族仇恨、破坏监管秩序罪等两个罪名增判<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年，与前罪合并执行<span lang="EN-US">20</span>年徒刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2038</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日止。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">益西曲珍（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">现年<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁，女，退休医生。因<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年在西藏首府拉萨协助救援受枪伤的示威藏人，遭到中共警方拘捕。同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被中共拉萨市中级人民法院以间谍罪判处<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年有期徒刑，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。法院方面在审判会上指出，益西曲珍接受西藏流亡政府安全部指派的任务及资助，向安全部提供危害国家安全及利益等方面的情报、信息，其行为已触犯中华人民共和国刑法第一百一十条的规定，构成间谍罪。藏人行政中央网站指出，正在西藏自治区第一监狱（又名：扎其监狱）中服刑的益西曲珍被捕后遭受警察刑讯逼供，并被关押在卫生条件极差、环境非常恶劣的监狱中，导致营养不良，疾病缠身。曾因身体状况极度恶化，被紧急送医。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">易家海：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖北省麻城市法轮功学员、<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年已经年过七旬，退休前是原麻城市乘马岗乡万义小学校长。因坚持修炼法轮功，多次被迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年曾被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，易家海、严英中，被当地中共恶警从家中抓捕，并关押在麻城市第一看守所一年多，于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年被秘密判刑：易家海被判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，严英中被判<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被关押到湖北省沙洋监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源： </b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/7/27/463465.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/7/27/463465.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">易文君：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1968</span>年出生，四川省成都市人，成都市青羊区牧电巷居民，资深职业画家，成都益州书画院前任常务理事，自由信仰追求者，法轮功信仰者，中国在押良心犯。早年曾于<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年开始锻炼法轮功，至<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，因时任中共最高领导人江泽民疯狂迫害、打压法轮功及其信仰者后，其曾因进京上访而被枉判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年；后因坚持自由信仰，且不畏风险，继续宣传法轮功而屡遭地方当局绑架和拘押，然而即便在此情形下，其仍创作出不少优秀画作，深受众人喜爱与好评；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，中共十九大前夕，其家突遭成都市武侯区红牌楼派出所和成都市青羊区草堂派出所两地警方的连手搜查，并于次日，其夫妇二人（其夫丁中斌，原系某高校及某高中物理教师，亦是法轮功信仰者）均被以涉嫌邪教罪刑拘，并关押至成都郫县看守所；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，因成都市青羊区检察院到郫县看守所“过检”，其夫妇才被以监视居住半年方式准予获释回家；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日—<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，其夫妇二人再被成都市青羊区草堂派出所警方刑拘，后其家遭查抄，家中新购的两台笔记本电脑、七部手机、多年珍藏价值不菲的自画作品、绘画所用的原材料及锻炼所用的法轮功书籍、个人上万元现金及银行卡等等均被洗劫一空；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，其夫因转为监视居住而获释放，而其则被青羊区警方以同罪由转正式逮捕；同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，其案被成都市青羊区检察院起诉至青羊区法院；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，被成都市青羊区法院一审以“组织和利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。目前在四川省女子监狱（四川省简阳市养马镇，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">641402</span>）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/12/8.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/12/8.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">尹峰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">济南市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日当天，济南市铁路派出所再次抓捕法轮功学员尹峰，警察同时对最近曾与尹峰有过交往的、居住在朝阳小区的法轮功学员程西江陈连美等法轮功学员抄家、抓捕。程西江被抄走打印机、电脑、大法书籍和一些《九评》、《共产主义的终极目的》等物品和书籍。当日下午，尹峰被逼交<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元保证金后回家。程西江、陈连美被关押在济南铁路看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被秘密审判，判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">尹兰华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，吉林辽源市龙山区柏林小镇法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日晚间<span lang="EN-US">9</span>点多，辽源市向阳公安分局警察郭凯明等人侵入尹兰华的家中，搜查大法书、法轮功资料、法轮功币。尹兰华也被抓捕到向阳公安分局。那里的警察将她双手反背，用铁铐子铐上<span lang="EN-US">3</span>天，对她刑讯逼供后，最后将尹兰华关押到辽源市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月尹兰华被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，并勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">尹旭安：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1974</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月出生，湖北省大冶市保安镇人，枉判上访者，公益维权者。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2015</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，因与王芳、耿彩文等人在武汉市黄鹤楼前身着声援屠夫（吴凎）的文化衫，并拍照上传网媒，随于<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被警方从家中带走，拘留于大冶市保安镇派出所，同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被转为刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”批捕，之后其案被大冶市检察院退补后又移送检察院审查起诉，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日审查起诉期满；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，其案在湖北省大冶市法院开庭受审。据悉，关押期间曾一直被拒绝律师会见，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日方获会见，知其遭狱警殴打虐待，导致身心伤害巨大。后被羁押于湖北省大冶市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年初才刑满获释。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，其又被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪“刑拘”；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，其案被大冶市检察院起诉至地方法院；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，其案被湖北省大冶市法院虽开庭审理，久拖至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日终被该法院以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日；据悉，其在狱中身体状况极差，已被抢救数次。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，湖北大冶看守所告诉尹家人：尹旭安因高血压偏高导致中风住院。尹旭安与父亲及哥哥视频会见后，家人反映尹现在说话口齿不清，基本生活不能自理，需要依靠其他人帮忙，家人心急如焚。尹旭安<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月底已被转入黄州监狱。目前在监狱医院住院，对比<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月份中风时情况有些好转，说话口齿比原来清晰一些，但是还是没有恢复到原来正常状态，脚也无法像原来那样正常行走，另外高血压在<span lang="EN-US">240</span>左右。现能自理，说话口齿不清，其身体情况令人担忧。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/02/blog-post_0.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast;">殷宝合：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁朝阳市两法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，殷宝合在恒屹家园粘真相贴时，被本小区内的刘宇恶告，朝阳北塔分局警察将殷宝合抓捕到北塔分局，并对殷宝合抄家。殷宝合被一直关押在朝阳市看守所。后殷宝合被北塔分局构陷到双塔区法院后，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日开庭。被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">应爱云：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">浙江丽水缙云县五云镇法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1947</span>年生。家住丽水市缙云县五云镇，因坚持修炼法轮大法，几次被中共人员抓捕，曾被劳教一年半及判刑三年半。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日（农历<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月十五中秋节）被抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月获知，已被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，目前还被关在丽水看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/12/18/453249.html"><b minor-fareast;">宁夏回族自治区中卫市中宁县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年生，男，原本是工程车司机。因修炼法轮功<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被中宁县法院判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日刑满释放。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日在中宁县被抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日被中宁县检察院批准逮捕，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，沙坡头区法院以枉判刑尤海军有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a lang="EN-US">1</span>家<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人后来被关押在宁河区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月初，检察院将构陷他们的案卷递交到宁河区法院刑事庭。近日获悉李国庆<span lang="EN-US">1</span>家<span lang="EN-US">3</span>口都被判刑。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月李国庆<span lang="EN-US">1</span>家<span lang="EN-US">3</span>口，被关押、构陷<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，王国辉被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。王国辉和于春丽当庭提出上诉。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">7</span>日在德惠市同太乡集市向民众宣传法轮功时，被同太派出所警察抓捕，后被关押到德惠市拘留所、看守所关押。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，于凤珍被法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，被关押到位于长春的吉林省女子监狱迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<b minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/10/2_65.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/10/18/%E5%90%89%E6%9E%97%E5%86%9C%E5%AE%89%E5%8E%BF%E4%BA%8E%E5%87%A4%E7%8F%8D%E3%80%81%E4%BA%8E%E6%B0%B8%E7%90%B4%E9%81%AD%E8%AF%AC%E5%88%A4%E8%A2%AB%E5%8A%AB%E6%8C%81%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1-467235.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/10/18/%E5%90%89%E6%9E%97%E5%86%9C%E5%AE%89%E5%8E%BF%E4%BA%8E%E5%87%A4%E7%8F%8D%E3%80%81%E4%BA%8E%E6%B0%B8%E7%90%B4%E9%81%AD%E8%AF%AC%E5%88%A4%E8%A2%AB%E5%8A%AB%E6%8C%81%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1-467235.html</span></b></a></span><b mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">于桂兰</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">：</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁抚顺市望花区法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1939</span>年生，现年<span lang="EN-US">82</span>岁。于桂兰老人一九九七年十月开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，在抚顺市顺城区葛布新地号，于桂兰告诉人们“法轮大法好，真善忍好”时，被人举报。于桂兰被前来的警车及举报人绑架。警察将于桂兰老人拉回派出所，晚上十点多，才让老人回家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，于桂兰老人去抚顺李石开发区发法轮功资料时，被望花雷锋派出所跟踪，绑架到望花雷锋派出所。四个月后，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日早上，望花区雷锋派出所警察到于桂兰家，让于桂兰到望花法院去一趟。于桂兰老人到了法院，法院人员将望花检察院对她的起诉书交给了于桂兰。于桂兰老人于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日在望花区法院第一法庭开庭。于桂兰老人被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，随即被强行关押在看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">于桂珍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吉林长春市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年生，女。<span lang="EN-US">1995</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，于桂珍开始修炼法轮功。于桂珍因坚持修炼法轮大法、修心向善，在中共对法轮功的持续迫害中，曾分别于<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年两次被长春市黑嘴子女子教养所关押，共计<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年多，她遭到毒打、电刑、体罚，她的胆被恶人打坏，前胸、后背身体组织损伤。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日晚<span lang="EN-US">9</span>点多，现居长春市的于桂珍，被绿园区西新派出所警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，于桂珍被关押到长春第四看守所<span lang="EN-US">202</span>监室，主管警察李琳。于桂珍被关押期间，绿园区西新派出所警察阻止律师接见。长春市绿园区、朝阳区公安、检察院、法院暗箱操作，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月份，于桂珍被朝阳区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">于华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吉林省长春市法轮功学员。于华、李维清<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日向人发放法轮功小册子，被跟踪，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日被义和路派出所抓捕、抄家，关押至长春市苇子沟拘留所。拘留十天之后，<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日早上被长春市朝阳分局和长春市义和路派出所劫持到长春市第四看守所关押至今。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，于华被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。于华提出上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日被长春市中级法院刑驳回上诉维持原判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/10/446035.html#227922208-1"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：于健莉一家七人法轮功案受害人之一。吉林长春市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，四平市公安局、梨树县公安局出动几百警力，包括四平市公安局国保大队、梨树县公安局国保大队、巡警、交警、梨树县辖区内各派出所警察，还调动所辖社区的部份人员，并在长春市当地警察的配合下，在长春市开始了对法轮功学员及其家属的绑架，并到在省内其它地区居住的学员及亲属家中进行绑架。于健莉一家七人在各自的家被公安警察绑架。包括：于健莉、母亲付贵华、丈夫王东吉、公公王克民、婆婆王凤芝、妹夫孟祥岐，及孟祥岐的父亲孟凡军。后一家七人均被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年至<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半，其中付贵华和孟祥岐被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半，其余<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人为<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: minor-fareast;">于娇茹：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1988</span>年生，长春市农安县法轮功学员。会计。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日清晨六点多钟，在农安县政府大楼对面，一群国保公安人员抓捕一家三口——蔡玉英、于娇茹母女，和这家老实巴交的男主人。那天，农安县非法抓捕了二十多名法轮功学员。此次非法抓捕行动，是由长春市政法委和农安县政法委共同策划实施的，长春市政法委书记马延峰亲赴农安县部署非法抓捕行动，七月十三日，农安县政法委、“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”召开会议落实具体行动方案。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日判决书下到看守所：于娇茹被判<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">于兰芳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New 0pt;">年生，家住山东省潍坊市高新区银通社区。近年在苏州市吴中区木渎镇女儿家帮忙带孩子。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，苏州市枫桥派出所警察闯到于兰芳的女儿家，抓捕了于兰芳。于兰芳在被关押<span lang="EN-US">36</span>天后，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月四日取保候审回家。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日下午，于兰芳女儿接到苏州市吴江区法院的电话通知，于兰芳的案子在<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日上午进行宣读判决书，告知在当日<span lang="EN-US">9</span>点<span lang="EN-US">50</span>分到达。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日上午，于兰芳与女儿准时到达法院，大概在十点多的时候，于兰芳被宣判，判决撤销之前缓刑，执行前次实刑判决，这次的判刑为<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，数罪并罚，扣除被关押时间，最终判决<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，被当庭扣押。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<u><span lang="EN-US">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/9/30/449621.html<o:p></o:p></span></u></b></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">于守芬：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，大连法轮功学员。于守芬<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日在付家庄海滩给带小孩玩的男子李鹏飞讲法轮功。结果李鹏飞打电话给西岗分局诬告，并把于守芬按倒在地，用腿压着于守芬胸部，直到警察到来，于守芬差点窒息过去。李鹏飞<span lang="EN-US">30</span>多岁，是西岗区公安分局便衣警察。当日，西岗分局和八一路派出所对于守芬抄家。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">2022</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被甘井子区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">4</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/11/3/451449.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/11/3/451449.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">于淑清：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吉林省榆树市五棵树镇法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年生，一九九六年春开始修炼法轮功，。中共<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年迫害法轮功后，她因坚持真善忍信仰，多次遭中共警察抓捕、关押，曾两次被劳教。于淑清<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日在滨江明月小区发放法轮功资料时遭人恶告，被榆树正阳派出所警察抓捕，关押在长春市看守所，后被德惠检察院批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月获悉，于淑清约于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月份被德惠法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/3/30/458292.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/3/30/458292.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">于艳华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江省安达市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1959</span>年生。于艳华在中共二十多年残酷迫害法轮功过程中，因坚持修炼法轮大法，多次被警察抓捕、关押。她曾三次被劳教，一次被判刑，共陷冤狱<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年。年迈婆婆在她关押期间悲伤离世，丈夫因营救她也遭中共判刑。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，于艳华在正阳街讲真相时被安达市公安局警察抓捕，先后被劫持到拘留所、看守所关押。后于艳华被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"> </span></b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/7/3/462589.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林省农安县法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1962</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日生，现年<span lang="EN-US">61</span>岁，家住吉林省农安县农安镇闫家村。一九九九年三月开始修炼法轮大法。后中共迫害法轮功后，于永琴多次遭到迫害。于永琴和于凤珍<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日在德惠市同太乡集市向民众宣传法轮功时，被同太派出所警察抓捕，后被关押到德惠市拘留所、看守所关押。期间于永琴因出现严重病症被保外就医。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，于凤珍被法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，被关押到位于长春的吉林省女子监狱迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/10/2_19.html"><b mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/10/18/%E5%90%89%E6%9E%97%E5%86%9C%E5%AE%89%E5%8E%BF%E4%BA%8E%E5%87%A4%E7%8F%8D%E3%80%81%E4%BA%8E%E6%B0%B8%E7%90%B4%E9%81%AD%E8%AF%AC%E5%88%A4%E8%A2%AB%E5%8A%AB%E6%8C%81%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1-467235.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">于云峰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">网名董狐直笔。生于<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年，是哈尔滨著名民主人士。多年来，他常直言不讳的抨击时政，也热心快肠的帮助民运人士。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，于云峰因言获罪被哈尔滨市当局判处劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，其《劳动教养决定书》写道：于云峰“<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日利用手机分别给哈市及外地市<span lang="EN-US">28</span>个手机用户，发送内容为反党反社会主义的短信，其目的是煽动颠覆国家政权，推翻社会主义制度，给社会稳定造成严重后果，严重扰乱社会治安”，“因其反党、反社会主义，根据《劳动教养试行办法》第十条第<span lang="EN-US">1</span>项的规定，决定对其劳动教养<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。”<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年，于云峰又因为在微信群转发谢阳律师受酷刑的消息，于两会前夕<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>号晚上<span lang="EN-US">6</span>点被抓进拘留所行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天。<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日到期还不放人，警方又说他诽谤毛泽东诽谤中国政府要再拘十天。于云峰、李佰华夫妇于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日遭哈尔滨市公安局香坊分局以“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留。本次夫妇一起被拘留具体事因未明。后于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月获悉于云峰、李佰华夫妇均被以寻衅滋事罪名，于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月（二审）被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，李佰华于<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月份已移送黑龙江女子监狱（集训队）服刑。于云峰目前还关押于哈尔滨香坊区看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/202012285.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">于珍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东齐鲁石化法轮功学员，女，齐鲁石化公司车辆管理中心客运四队司机，<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年开始修炼法轮功。于珍女士于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月底被齐都公安局北区分局经常抓捕，后被中共法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。于珍目前被关押在哪里不得而知。有消息称，她遭抓捕迫害的原因可能是她在网上通过<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个软件讲法轮功或者是和同修学法交流。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/1/12/454797.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/1/12/454797.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">余爱明：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">福清市访民。余爱眀因为在<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日到福州大酒店找驻闽的中央巡视组，当场被地方政府的截访维稳人员抓走失联。余爱明的儿子得知信息后，向福州市公安局报了警。今天，余爱明的儿子收到福州市公安局安泰派出所出具的受案回执，告知余爱明已被“人民”政府送到福乐园精神病医院，也就是非法拘禁了。据了解，在福建省福州市，因为认为自己合法权益受到不法侵害，而信访维权被囚禁精神病院迫害的有肢体残疾人雷忠林，具有硕士文凭的叶钟，还有已经被囚禁两年多至今未获自由的何观娇、及晋安区的叶明峰、马尾区的朱晚秀、福清市的陈道财、）刘金云，魏英，陈梅云等，据说实际被非法拘禁于精神病院的访民人数达数十人之多。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/08/blog-post_81.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/08/blog-post_81.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">余德贞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">宁夏石嘴山市惠农区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，余德贞、史梅兰、陈秀萍在石嘴山市惠农区水城民生片区讲法轮功，贴真相不干胶，被国保大队和园艺派出所便衣警察跟踪抓捕、抄家，当晚三人被放回家。此后，警察便对每位法轮功学员进行暗中监控和跟踪。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，余德贞、史梅兰、陈秀萍、刘翠梅等人被国保警察有预谋的抓捕、抄家。刘翠梅是从银川市的家中被警察抓捕到石嘴山市惠农区，在审讯过程中，多次被殴打。当天，余德贞、陈秀萍、史梅兰、刘翠梅被“取保候审”回家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，余德贞、史梅兰、陈秀萍、刘翠梅再被抓捕，在石嘴山看守所被关押。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，余德贞、陈秀萍、史美兰、刘翠梅被石嘴山市大武口区法院判刑。余德贞被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，被罚金三万元；陈秀萍被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，被罚金二万五千元；史梅兰被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，被罚金一万元；刘翠梅被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，被罚金一万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">余凤连：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川宜宾珙县访民。余凤连是因为父亲余大同在</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1952</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年的土地改革时，划分获得了一块山林，父亲去世后，由余凤连和哥哥继承。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2004</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年，余凤连发现自己的山林被相邻的五星村村民余兴伍的继承人侵占，就根据“森林法”规定，向下罗乡政府、珙县政府提起反映，请求调查处理，但政府部门一直没有处理。直到</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">5</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年后，珙县政府于</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2009</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年作出</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">“关于对下罗乡梧桐村四社余友堂与五星村五社武兴菊林权证争议的决定”，余凤连兄妹不服，向宜宾市政府申请复议，被驳回，上诉至宜宾市中级法院，同样被驳回，最后只能走上所谓“信访不信法”之路。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">9</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">28</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日上午，余凤连，在位于北京东城区东堂子胡同</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">49-1</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">号公安部信访接待室上访，被地方截访</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">5-6</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">个便衣公安强制拷上手铐，以“通辑犯”为名抓捕。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">9</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">30</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日余凤连的家属收到珙县公安局以“涉嫌寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留的通知书。<b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">余光河</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：重庆市人，重庆市巴南区李家沱居民，法轮功学员。因信仰和宣传法轮功信息，长期遭重庆市巴南区当局骚扰、跟踪、劳教等迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，余光河突然被重庆市九龙坡区国保警察抓走，家被查抄，后得知因宣传法轮功信息被以涉邪教罪刑拘，关押在九龙坡区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日其被重庆市九龙坡区法院开庭受审，并被一审以“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”枉法判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年。其不服判决，立即提出上诉，但二审仍然维持原判。目前在重庆市永川监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">余红：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">重庆九龙坡区法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1954</span>年生，家住重庆市九龙坡区杨家坪街道。因修炼法轮功，曾两次被中共法院判刑，关押<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日上午，河南省商水县国保警察，伙同重庆南岸区大佛寺派出所警察闯入余红住处，抄家四个多小时，抢走电脑、<span lang="EN-US">U</span>盘等物品，并抓捕余红，把她关押在重庆看守所。据悉，河南和重庆警察怀疑余红上明慧网曝光河南省商水县警察抓捕重庆法轮功学员余秀容的恶行，而抓捕余红。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，九龙坡区法院对余红判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"> </span></b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/6/458517.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/6/458517.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">余洪英</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：四川省西昌市</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">1963</span><span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">年生，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁，攀西地质大队退休职工。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，余洪英在西昌市大巷口邮局门口，被西昌市公安局国保、西昌市铁路公安处国保及派出所警察抓捕，并抄家。</span><span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，成都铁路运输第二法院，一同到西昌市看守所，对六旬的余洪英宣判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/6/17/462057.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/6/17/462057.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">余慧明</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：女，<span lang="EN-US">1987</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日出生，英文名：<span lang="EN-US">Winnie,Yu Wai Ming</span>，原英属香港籍、现中华人民共和国（香港）籍人，前香港医管局医疗信息部助理行政主任，前香港医管局内科护士、深切治疗部护士，前香港医管局总部<span lang="EN-US">IT</span>部职员，香港医管局员工阵线主席，泛民主派人士，民主派初选案（又称“<span lang="EN-US">47</span>人初选案”）被告之一、中国在押政治犯。早年曾就读于香港中文大学医学院护理系；毕业后，<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-2014</span>年，曾在香港医管局任职内科护士，后又转到深切治疗部任职；并曾言“不理世事”和时事；但自从<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年香港占领行动（又称“雨伞运动”）以来，尤其是<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日香港政府向抗议市民投下了催泪弹，其开始意识到关心社会时政的必要性；后又因<span lang="EN-US"> 2020</span>年香港《逃犯条例》修订引发了百万人大游行，再次促其对社会议题更多关注，随毅然与其他医护人员筹组工会，并出任工会组织主席；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年，曾因不满医管局管理层无视在改用电子派药系统时出现漏洞而使其同事被迫辞职，以及系统人手不足等问题，而申请调职到总部的<span lang="EN-US">IT</span>部任职，以期了解改良一个电子系统的难度，从而更好地在体制中推动改革；曾因<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年冠状病毒疫情在香港蔓延，进而引发相关医护事宜的争议，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，其随发起医护人员大罢工，并于同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，又代表卫生服务界参与立法会民主派初选（官方又称“<span lang="EN-US">35+</span>初选”）；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，其与<span lang="EN-US">40</span>余名泛民主派人士统一被香港国安处警方以涉嫌“串谋颠覆国家政权罪”拘捕；被控此前因参选立法会民主派区域选举，故而触犯了香港国安法规定；同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，其又被香港高等法院批准保释，但至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，因其保释期间在<span lang="EN-US">Facebook</span>（脸书）上发布帖文，被香港当局认为危害国家安全及违反法院的保释条件，遂再次在香港沙田区被收监逮捕；次日，即被西九龙裁判法院撤销保释，并要求再押侯审。目前疑被羁押于荔枝角收押所。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/04/blog-post_45.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/04/blog-post_45.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> </span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">余江帆：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1989</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日出生，女，河南省南阳市籍人，河南省邓州市夏集乡杨河移民村公民，维权访民，人称“访二代”，人权捍卫者，中国在押维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年，余江帆因支持南水北调西线工程，随其全家从原籍河南省淅川县香花镇搬迁至河南省邓州市夏集乡移民村；搬迁后，<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年，因发现移民安置房存有重大质量安全隐患问题，余江帆随其父与多位村民前往省政府投诉，讨说法，不料却被当地警方带回，后被以“上访带头人”之名遭拘押、训诫及殴打，不久含恨去世；为完成父亲遗愿，其自此成了“访二代”，并多次依法逐级投诉表达要求，但毫无果效反遭严打；曾<span lang="EN-US">11</span>次被邓州市警方以 “扰乱公共秩序”罪由行政拘留十数日；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年，再次被邓州市警方行政拘留后又转刑事拘留，至<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，被河南省邓州市法院以“寻衅滋事罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，之后在郑州女子监狱服刑；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，刑满出狱；之后，其为谋生计而前往北京打工，但因其又积极参与北京地区的公民维权活动（如公民聚餐、声援关注良心犯等活动），故频遭北京警方的逼迫打压；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，曾<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次被邓州市警方以“扰乱单位<span lang="EN-US">/</span>公共场所秩序”为由各处行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年，曾因其与地方政府就村民房屋修缮问题未达成一致（即拒绝地方当局仅就其个人房屋修缮问题提出解决方案，坚持要求政府先对全村<span lang="EN-US">295</span>户房屋进行质量评估，按照评估结果凭现金发放给各户自行修缮，完毕后再解决自己的房屋问题），遂再遭强力打压；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，余江帆在河北活动时，再被赶来的邓州市维稳人员拉走遣返，之后先被邓州市警方处行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">18</span>天；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，又被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”转正式刑拘，并被送南阳市看守所羁押；同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，被邓州市检察院以同罪名予以批捕，指控其之前的在京上访行为有违国家法律，又是累犯，故建议法院应予从重处罚；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，余江帆案在河南省邓州市法院开庭审理，但庭审中因检察院控其三起上访行为均发生在北京，且其一直常驻北京，故而河南省邓州市法院根本无管辖权，其案长时被迫休庭；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被邓州市法院以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日；然而，当其刑期获释日并未被获释，理由是邓州市法院以其上诉南阳市中级法院裁定案件发回重审为由，拒绝对其（以取保候审）予以释放；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，河南省邓州市法院以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。目前羁押于河南省南阳市看守所。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/09/246.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/09/246.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">余浚聪：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">深圳佳士工人。因要求组建独立工会，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被深圳警方以寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留，同时被刑事拘留的有<span lang="EN-US">14</span>名工人。关押在深圳龙岗区看守所。关押两年未有信息。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">余钱：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1986</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日出生，湖北省鄂州市人，鄂州市鄂城区泽林镇兴桥村公民，曾在上海工作，基督徒，网络活跃人士，推特常用账号“余钱<span lang="EN-US">100 @tianfushiming</span>”，民主人士，人权捍卫者，中国在押政治犯。早年因家境贫寒，遍尝人间疾苦，长大后曾在上海工作；曾因极富正义感，在工作之余曾多次痛批高层领导目无法治，并在推特上自称“既是冲塔的坦克人，亦是湖北的李文亮”，故使得上海市和湖北省鄂州市相关高层领导极度不满，将其定为急需维稳监控的打压对象；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，曾因纪念六四<span lang="EN-US">21</span>周年而禁食祈祷并发绝食短信，两天后遂被上海市奉贤区江海派出所警方以涉嫌“扰乱公共秩序”罪由传唤，并处行政处罚<span lang="EN-US">200</span>元；后其不服处罚决定，随即发起行政复议决定，将上海市奉贤区政府告上上海市第一中级法院，以期该法院裁决撤销对其的行政处罚；之后其被迫返回湖北老家生活，此期间，因仍持续发声，揭批鄂州市贪腐官商勾结、遍地黑厂、癌症村、打黑运动、机场圈地强拆三万户、政府行政造假等问题，故被鄂州市警方在其老家村里沿路电线杆上布满摄像头；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，曾因湖北省长王忠林到鄂州市指导疫情防控，官方虽称实施封控范围只限鄂州中心城区约<span lang="EN-US">30</span>万人，但各乡镇立即在省长指示下以乡镇名义发布鄂州市整体静态管理通知，实际封控多达近百万人；对此，其遂网发诘问：各乡镇在没有合法文件情况下非法额外封控<span lang="EN-US">70</span>万民众，非法拘禁街上民众并送集中强制学习是否合情合法；因其网络异议立引社会热议，遂于同年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日和<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日先后三次被以“寻衅滋事”或“境外推特发帖和恶意抹黑中国政府和中国共产党”为罪由传唤，并且第三次传唤时，一无传唤证，二被关小黑屋<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个多小时，三还被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，因其再次在推特上发布评论中国政府和中国共产党的文图资讯，故而让湖北当局十分恼火，遂派当地警方在其住宅四周又安装上新的监控摄像头，以进行全天候居家监控，且再遭几次“寻衅滋事“罪由传唤；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">因其对此不服，故而于同月先后两次向鄂州市华容区法院发起行政复议和行政起诉状，但无果；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，因余钱再次向鄂州市中级法院起诉，并发布推文“六四发声无罪，监听公民通信才有罪”；遂被鄂州市鄂城区泽林派出所警方迅速抓走，自此失联；拘押至今，一直未放。目前被羁押地点不明。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/01/blog-post_67.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/01/blog-post_67.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">余荣新：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广东省江门市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日余荣新被抓捕，关押在江门市看守所，他的妻子谢清约在<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被抓捕，也被关押在江门市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，在未通知律师和家属的情况下，广东江门法院秘密判刑，余荣新被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年半，妻子谢清被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半。余荣新刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">余绍萍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1950</span>年代生人，四川成都市大邑县原北街小学教师、法轮功学员<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日中午，余绍萍被大邑县公安局晋原镇派出所警察抓捕，一行五、六个人，一进校门，就开始摄像，校长在门口接待，并指余绍萍的住房。后被抓捕。余绍萍被关押在郫县看守所。于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日在大邑县法院被开庭，余绍萍判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并被勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/27/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E5%9B%9B%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%83%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-441694.html"><b mso-hansi-theme-font:
