class="MsoHyperlink"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">余素芳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河南省信阳市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1950</span>年生，女，河南省信阳市潢川县人。她于一九九八年开始修炼法轮功。在中共对法轮功的迫害中，余素芳坚持信仰，几次被中共抓捕、关押，曾被判刑四年，在新乡女子监狱遭受迫害。余素芳于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被信阳市潢川县公安局一帮便衣警察抓捕、抄家抢劫、构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被潢川县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金一万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/21/459042.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/21/459042.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">余文生：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1967</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日出生，北京市人，前北京市隆聚律师事务所主任、前北京市律师协会青年委员会委员，原北京市道衡律师事务所律师，北京知名人权律师。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年，曾因为中国奥运的知识产权事宜付出了巨大努力，而荣获北京市律师协会颁发的“律师行业奥运工作突出贡献奖”；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年，曾被评为北京市石景山律协律师代表；近年来，曾因高度关注弱势群体，为多起维权案件当事人作过代理律师（如基督徒徐彩虹、何斌案、王春艳姊妹敲诈政府案，浙江维权代表朱瑛娣案，李英之案，拆迁上访者赵勇案，著名律师王成诉律协和法制日报案等），而受到业界及维权群体的普遍好评和欢迎；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，因前往黑龙江省牡丹江市看守所要求会见当事人（即被关押的法轮功信仰者），而被警方非法抓进看守所；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，因前往监狱迎接因要求官员财产公示而获刑的维权公民袁冬出狱，而遭到当局的再次不满；同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，因前往预约会见因声援香港占中事件被羁押于北京市丰台看守所的维权公民张宗钢，遭到拒绝后将实情发到网上，遂于又一次遭到当局的强烈不满和恶意打击，<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日即被北京市警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事”刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，被北京市大兴区检察院以同罪名予以批捕；其妻曾先后委托<span lang="EN-US">8</span>名律师近<span lang="EN-US">20</span>次要求会见余文生，均被当局以“需要向市局汇报、案件涉及国家秘密”为由拒绝，直至<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，终获取保释放；获释后，曾遭多次当局骚扰和暗示，令其不能正常找到工作；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，因此前在看守所时患上小肠疝气，又受到狱警酷刑虐待及饥饿折磨，其随向北京市大兴区检察院正式提出要求国家赔偿申请，孰料<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日却等来一份来自北京市司法局注销其律师资格证的决定书；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，被北京市石景山警方以涉嫌“妨碍公务罪”再次刑拘，关押于石景山看守所；同年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，又被江苏省徐州市铜山区警方以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”指定居所监视居住；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，被徐州市警方以同罪名正式逮捕，并被羁押于徐州市看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，其案在徐州市中级法院秘密开庭，但久拖不判；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，终被该法院一审以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”秘判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年；其不服上诉；二审依然维持原判；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，刑满释放；据悉，狱中其身患严重慢性疾病，长期医治无效，又因双手颤抖残疾愈加严重，故其生活难以自理。此前在江苏省南京监狱老残监区服刑。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，余文生及其妻子许艳被刑事拘留，罪名是“寻衅滋事”。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日晚，超过<span lang="EN-US">7</span>名警察到余文生的住处，向其刚满<span lang="EN-US">18</span>岁的儿子宣读余文生律师及其妻子许艳被刑事拘留的通知，不给书面文件也不允许拍照。众警察还对家里进行了搜查，在未出具任何搜查文书的情况下带走一些私人物品。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/04/blog-post_24.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/04/blog-post_24.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">宇美霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日出生，山东省昌乐县法轮功学员。家住昌乐县五图镇，是昌乐县第<span lang="EN-US">3</span>职业中专高级教师。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，宇美霞曾被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，并被罚款<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，宇美霞冤狱期满，回到家中，她的退休工资被社保局停发。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日因她继续宣传法轮大法，遭城关派出所抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日她在青州法院被视频开庭，被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/1/441950.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/1/441950.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">俞涛：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东茂名市高州市法轮功学员，优秀教师、一九七七年出生，广州大学本科毕业后，入伍两年。后在高州市大井镇第一中学任数学等理科教学。俞涛于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月被高州市国保大队、城南派出所警察抓捕、关押构陷。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，他被茂南区检察院构陷到法院，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月，罚金一万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://big5.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/8/23/%E5%BB%A3%E6%9D%B1%E8%8C%82%E5%90%8D%E9%AB%98%E5%B7%9E%E5%84%AA%E7%A7%80%E6%95%99%E5%B8%AB%E4%BF%9E%E6%BF%A4%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-464495.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">喻颖祝：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖南省株洲市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1974</span>年生，原株洲冶炼厂职工，家住株洲市石峰区清水塘沈家湾社区。因坚持修炼法轮功，在中共对法轮功持续<span lang="EN-US">24</span>年的迫害中，曾三次被劳教，共计入狱七年。喻颖祝于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，她在家中被当地警察抓捕，后被关押至长沙市第四看守所。喻颖祝绝食抵制迫害两个月，身体非常虚弱，人瘦得皮包骨。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，喻颖祝被释放回家，被“监视居住”。<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日下午，喻颖祝再次在家中被雨花区法院指使的警察抓捕、又被关押在长沙市第四看守所。<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，雨花区法院在第五审判庭对喻颖祝进行庭审，对喻颖祝判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/09/3_29.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/09/3_29.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/9/15/%E6%9B%BE%E9%81%AD%E5%86%A4%E7%8B%B1%E4%B8%83%E5%B9%B4-%E6%B9%96%E5%8D%97%E6%A0%AA%E6%B4%B2%E5%96%BB%E9%A2%96%E7%A5%9D%E5%A5%B3%E5%A3%AB%E5%8F%88%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4-465324.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/9/15/%E6%9B%BE%E9%81%AD%E5%86%A4%E7%8B%B1%E4%B8%83%E5%B9%B4-%E6%B9%96%E5%8D%97%E6%A0%AA%E6%B4%B2%E5%96%BB%E9%A2%96%E7%A5%9D%E5%A5%B3%E5%A3%AB%E5%8F%88%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4-465324.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">袁华秀：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">四川成都法轮功学员，女<b>。</b></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">袁华秀于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被恶警抓捕，关押<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年后家属也没接到开庭通知，后来才知道袁华秀于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被成都高新区法院、检察院黑箱操作，判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。袁华秀不服冤判，提出上诉。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<u><span lang="EN-US">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/14/446234.html</span></u><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">袁王柱：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">湖北省黄冈市黄梅县法轮功学员。湖北省黄梅县大河镇花园山村人，生于<span lang="EN-US">1952</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年，袁王柱修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，袁王柱在发法轮功资料过程中，被村干诬告，遭大河镇派出所及黄梅县国保抓捕，后在黄冈市的武穴市法院被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，如今被关押在湖北省沙洋农场范家台九监遭受迫害。<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/21/%E6%B9%96%E5%8C%97%E9%BB%84%E6%A2%85%E5%8E%BF%E4%B8%83%E6%97%AC%E8%A2%81%E7%8E%8B%E6%9F%B1%E8%A2%AB%E5%86%A4%E5%88%A4%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-441531.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/21/%E6%B9%96%E5%8C%97%E9%BB%84%E6%A2%85%E5%8E%BF%E4%B8%83%E6%97%AC%E8%A2%81%E7%8E%8B%E6%9F%B1%E8%A2%AB%E5%86%A4%E5%88%A4%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-441531.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">袁文格：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北省石家庄市深泽县法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1946</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">77</span>岁。家住石家庄市深泽县留村乡李家庄村，她于<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，袁文格被深泽县公安局白庄乡派出所警察从家中抓捕，关押到石家庄市第二看守所迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日获悉：袁文格已被石家庄晋州市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/6/23/462263.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/6/23/462263.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 159.5pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">袁志强：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">重庆北碚区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，在北碚区居民住宅小区几处出现法轮功真相粘贴，当地警察怀疑是由袁志强提供，另一女性法轮功学员粘贴的。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，北碚区国保支队警察，闯进袁志强位于北碚区东阳街道磨心坡村的家中，抄走了大法书籍、真相数据和计算机、打印机等物品。袁志强被关押在北碚区三溪口看守所。后得知，袁志强被江北区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">岳春光：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林通化市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日晚上，通化市二道江区法轮功学员潘洪明、岳春光等四人在岳春光家学习法轮功书籍，遭二道江区公安分局、国保大队、山下派出所、社区等人员抓捕。后潘洪明被关押到通化市看守所，岳春光被关押到柳河县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月他们相继被庭审，大概在六、七月间被秘密判刑：潘洪明被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，岳春光<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。岳春光刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/09/32.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/09/32.html</span></b></a></span><b minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">岳乃亮：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1960</span>年生。家住吉林省吉林市昌邑区莲花街。他和妻子焦秀萍、弟弟岳乃明因坚持修炼法轮功，多次遭中共人员抓捕、关押，焦秀萍、岳乃明都曾被劳教两年，岳乃明在<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年被抓捕后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半。岳乃亮在<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日在丰满区建华村的母亲家被华山路派出所警察抓捕，先被拘留十五天，之后被关押在口前看守所，又转到吉林市看守所一年半，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月末被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，目前已被关押到四平监狱。警察当时抓捕岳乃亮的所谓“理由”是，他在母亲家粘贴了“法轮功好、真善忍好”内容的对联、年画和福字等。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 159.5pt;"><span lang="EN-US"><a
